                }\n
\n
                $clientRepo = new Repository(Client::class);\n
                $client = $clientRepo->getByAttributes(['siret' => $siret], false);\n
\n
                if (!$client) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Client not found');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Mise à jour des champs client\n
                if (isset($inputData['companyName'])) {\n
                    $client->setCompanyName($inputData['companyName']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['workfield'])) {\n
                    $client->setWorkfield($inputData['workfield']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['contactFirstname'])) {\n
                    $client->setContactFirstname($inputData['contactFirstname']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['contactLastname'])) {\n
                    $client->setContactLastname($inputData['contactLastname']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['contactEmail'])) {\n
                    $client->setContactEmail($inputData['contactEmail']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['contactPhone'])) {\n
                    $client->setContactPhone($inputData['contactPhone']);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Sauvegarde client avec requête personnalisée car la clé primaire est siret (string)\n
                $clientSpecificRepo = new ClientRepository();\n
                $clientSpecificRepo->updateBySiret($client, $siret);\n
\n
                // Mise à jour ou création de l'adresse\n
                $addressData  = $inputData['address'] ?? null;\n
                $addressArray = null;\n
\n
                if ($addressData && !empty($addressData['streetNumber']) && !empty($addressData['streetName']) && !empty($addressData['postCode']) && !empty($addressData['city'])) {\n
                    $existingAddressId = $clientSpecificRepo->findExistingAddressId($siret);\n
\n
                    $addressFields = [\n
                        'streetnumber' => (int) $addressData['streetNumber'],\n
                        'streetletter' => $addressData['streetLetter'] ?? null,\n
                        'streetname'   => $addressData['streetName'],\n
                        'postcode'     => $addressData['postCode'],\n
                        'state'        => $addressData['state'] ?? null,\n
                        'city'         => $addressData['city'],\n
                        'country'      => $addressData['country'] ?? null,\n
                    ];\n
\n
                    if ($existingAddressId !== null) {\n
                        // Mise à jour de l'adresse existante\n
                        $clientSpecificRepo->updateAddress($existingAddressId, $addressFields);\n
                        $addressArray = array_merge(['id' => $existingAddressId], [\n
                            'streetNumber' => (int) $addressData['streetNumber'],\n
                            'streetLetter' => $addressData['streetLetter'] ?? null,\n
                            'streetName'   => $addressData['streetName'],\n
                            'postCode'     => $addressData['postCode'],\n
                            'state'        => $addressData['state'] ?? null,\n
                            'city'         => $addressData['city'],\n
                            'country'      => $addressData['country'] ?? null,\n
                        ]);\n

                        // Créer une nouvelle adresse\n

                        $address->setStreetName($addressData['streetName']);\n

                        $address->setState($addressData['state'] ?? null);\n
                        $address->setCity($addressData['city']);\n
                        $address->setCountry($addressData['country'] ?? null);\n

    /**\n
     * API GET /api/clients/search?q=terme\n
     * Recherche dynamique de clients par raison sociale, SIRET ou secteur.\n
     */\n
    final public function sirenLookup(): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Méthode non autorisée', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $q = trim($_GET['q'] ?? '');\n
\n
        if ($q === '' || !ctype_digit($q)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Numéro invalide : seuls les chiffres sont acceptés', 400);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $apiKey = $_ENV['SIREN_API_KEY'] ?? '';\n
\n
        if (strlen($q) <= 9) {\n
            $url = "https://data.siren-api.fr/v3/unites_legales/{$q}";\n
        } else {\n
            $url = "https://data.siren-api.fr/v3/etablissements/{$q}";\n
        }\n
\n
        $context = stream_context_create([\n
            'http' => [\n
                'method'        => 'GET',\n
                'header'        => "X-Client-Secret: {$apiKey}\r\nAccept: application/json\r\n",\n
                'ignore_errors' => true,\n
                'timeout'       => 10,\n
            ],\n
        ]);\n
\n
        $response = @file_get_contents($url, false, $context);\n
\n
        $httpCode = 200;\n
        if (isset($http_response_header)) {\n
            foreach ($http_response_header as $header) {\n
                if (preg_match('/HTTP\/\S+ (\d+)/', $header, $matches)) {\n
                    $httpCode = (int) $matches[1];\n
                }\n
            }\n
        }\n
\n
        if ($response === false || $httpCode === 503) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Impossible de contacter l\'API SIREN', 503);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if ($httpCode === 404) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Entreprise non trouvée', 404);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $data = json_decode($response, true);\n
\n
        if ($httpCode !== 200 || !$data) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Erreur lors de la récupération des données', 500);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $normalized = [];\n
\n
        if (isset($data['unite_legale'])) {\n
            $ul = $data['unite_legale'];\n
            $denomination = $ul['denomination'] ?? null;\n
            if (!$denomination && isset($ul['nom'])) {\n
                $denomination = trim(($ul['prenom_usuel'] ?? '') . ' ' . $ul['nom']);\n
            }\n
            $normalized['companyName'] = $denomination;\n
            $normalized['workfield']   = $ul['activite_principale'] ?? null;\n
\n
            if (isset($ul['etablissement_siege'])) {\n
                $siege = $ul['etablissement_siege'];\n
                $normalized['streetNumber'] = $siege['numero_voie'] ?? null;\n
                $normalized['streetLetter'] = $siege['indice_repetition'] ?? null;\n
                $streetType = $siege['type_voie'] ?? '';\n
                $streetLabel = $siege['libelle_voie'] ?? '';\n
                $normalized['streetName'] = trim($streetType . ' ' . $streetLabel) ?: null;\n
                $normalized['postCode']   = $siege['code_postal'] ?? null;\n
                $normalized['city']       = $siege['libelle_commune'] ?? null;\n
                $normalized['country']    = 'France';\n
            }\n
        } elseif (isset($data['etablissement'])) {\n
            $etab = $data['etablissement'];\n
            $ul   = $etab['unite_legale'] ?? [];\n
            $denomination = $ul['denomination'] ?? ($etab['enseigne_1'] ?? ($etab['denomination_usuelle'] ?? null));\n
            $normalized['companyName']  = $denomination;\n
            $normalized['workfield']    = $etab['activite_principale'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['streetNumber'] = $etab['numero_voie'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['streetLetter'] = $etab['indice_repetition'] ?? null;\n
            $streetType = $etab['type_voie'] ?? '';\n
            $streetLabel = $etab['libelle_voie'] ?? '';\n
            $normalized['streetName'] = trim($streetType . ' ' . $streetLabel) ?: null;\n
            $normalized['postCode']   = $etab['code_postal'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['city']       = $etab['libelle_commune'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['country']    = 'France';\n
        }\n
\n
        $this->jsonSuccess($normalized);\n
    }\n
\n
    final public function searchApiClients(): void\n
    {\n
        try {\n
            $searchTerm = trim($_GET['q'] ?? '');\n
            $clientRepo = new ClientRepository();\n
\n
            if ($searchTerm === '') {\n
                $clients     = $clientRepo->getAll();\n
                $clientsData = $clients ? array_map(fn ($c) => $c->toArray(), $clients) : [];\n
                $this->jsonSuccess(['clients' => $clientsData, 'total' => count($clientsData)]);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $rawRows = $clientRepo->searchByTerm($searchTerm);\n
\n
            $clientsData = array_map(function (array $row) {\n
                return [\n
                    'siret'            => $row['siret'],\n
                    'companyName'      => $row['companyname'],\n
                    'workfield'        => $row['workfield'],\n
                    'contactFirstname' => $row['contactfirstname'],\n
                    'contactLastname'  => $row['contactlastname'],\n
                    'contactEmail'     => $row['contactemail'],\n
                    'contactPhone'     => $row['contactphone'] ?? null,\n
                ];\n
            }, $rawRows);\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['clients' => $clientsData, 'total' => count($clientsData)]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage());\n
        }\n
    }\n

    final public function addApiClient(): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n

            try {\n
                // Récupération des données JSON\n
                $inputData = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true);\n
\n
                if (!$inputData) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('No data received');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validation des champs obligatoires\n
                if (empty($inputData['siret'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('SIRET number is required');\n
                }\n
                if (empty($inputData['companyName'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Company name is required');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validation du format SIRET (14 caractères)\n
                if (14 !== \strlen($inputData['siret']) || !ctype_digit($inputData['siret'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('SIRET number must be exactly 14 digits');\n
                }\n
\n
                $clientRepo = new Repository(Client::class);\n
\n
                // Vérifier si le client existe déjà\n
                $existingClient = $clientRepo->getByAttributes(['siret' => $inputData['siret']], false);\n
                if ($existingClient) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('A client with this SIRET number already exists');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Création du client\n
                $client = new Client();\n
                $client->setSiret($inputData['siret']);\n
                $client->setCompanyName($inputData['companyName']);\n
                $client->setWorkfield($inputData['workfield'] ?? null);\n
                $client->setContactFirstname($inputData['contactFirstname'] ?? null);\n
                $client->setContactLastname($inputData['contactLastname'] ?? null);\n
                $client->setContactEmail($inputData['contactEmail'] ?? null);\n

                        'postcode'     => $addressData['postCode'],\n

                        'city'         => $addressData['city'],\n
                        'country'      => $addressData['country'] ?? null,\n

    /**\n
     * API GET /api/clients/search?q=terme\n
     * Recherche dynamique de clients par raison sociale, SIRET ou secteur.\n
     */\n
    final public function sirenLookup(): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Méthode non autorisée', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $q = trim($_GET['q'] ?? '');\n
\n
        if ($q === '' || !ctype_digit($q)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Numéro invalide : seuls les chiffres sont acceptés', 400);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $apiKey = $_ENV['SIREN_API_KEY'] ?? '';\n
\n
        if (strlen($q) <= 9) {\n
            $url = "https://data.siren-api.fr/v3/unites_legales/{$q}";\n
        } else {\n
            $url = "https://data.siren-api.fr/v3/etablissements/{$q}";\n
        }\n
\n
        $context = stream_context_create([\n
            'http' => [\n
                'method'        => 'GET',\n
                'header'        => "X-Client-Secret: {$apiKey}\r\nAccept: application/json\r\n",\n
                'ignore_errors' => true,\n
                'timeout'       => 10,\n
            ],\n
        ]);\n
\n
        $response = @file_get_contents($url, false, $context);\n
\n
        $httpCode = 200;\n
        if (isset($http_response_header)) {\n
            foreach ($http_response_header as $header) {\n
                if (preg_match('/HTTP\/\S+ (\d+)/', $header, $matches)) {\n
                    $httpCode = (int) $matches[1];\n
                }\n
            }\n
        }\n
\n
        if ($response === false || $httpCode === 503) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Impossible de contacter l\'API SIREN', 503);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if ($httpCode === 404) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Entreprise non trouvée', 404);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $data = json_decode($response, true);\n
\n
        if ($httpCode !== 200 || !$data) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Erreur lors de la récupération des données', 500);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $normalized = [];\n
\n
        if (isset($data['unite_legale'])) {\n
            $ul = $data['unite_legale'];\n
            $denomination = $ul['denomination'] ?? null;\n
            if (!$denomination && isset($ul['nom'])) {\n
                $denomination = trim(($ul['prenom_usuel'] ?? '') . ' ' . $ul['nom']);\n
            }\n
            $normalized['companyName'] = $denomination;\n
            $normalized['workfield']   = $ul['activite_principale'] ?? null;\n
\n
            if (isset($ul['etablissement_siege'])) {\n
                $siege = $ul['etablissement_siege'];\n
                $normalized['streetNumber'] = $siege['numero_voie'] ?? null;\n
                $normalized['streetLetter'] = $siege['indice_repetition'] ?? null;\n
                $streetType = $siege['type_voie'] ?? '';\n
                $streetLabel = $siege['libelle_voie'] ?? '';\n
                $normalized['streetName'] = trim($streetType . ' ' . $streetLabel) ?: null;\n
                $normalized['postCode']   = $siege['code_postal'] ?? null;\n
                $normalized['city']       = $siege['libelle_commune'] ?? null;\n
                $normalized['country']    = 'France';\n
            }\n
        } elseif (isset($data['etablissement'])) {\n
            $etab = $data['etablissement'];\n
            $ul   = $etab['unite_legale'] ?? [];\n
            $denomination = $ul['denomination'] ?? ($etab['enseigne_1'] ?? ($etab['denomination_usuelle'] ?? null));\n
            $normalized['companyName']  = $denomination;\n
            $normalized['workfield']    = $etab['activite_principale'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['streetNumber'] = $etab['numero_voie'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['streetLetter'] = $etab['indice_repetition'] ?? null;\n
            $streetType = $etab['type_voie'] ?? '';\n
            $streetLabel = $etab['libelle_voie'] ?? '';\n
            $normalized['streetName'] = trim($streetType . ' ' . $streetLabel) ?: null;\n
            $normalized['postCode']   = $etab['code_postal'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['city']       = $etab['libelle_commune'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['country']    = 'France';\n
        }\n
\n
        $this->jsonSuccess($normalized);\n
    }\n
\n
    final public function searchApiClients(): void\n
    {\n
        try {\n
            $searchTerm = trim($_GET['q'] ?? '');\n
            $clientRepo = new ClientRepository();\n
\n
            if ($searchTerm === '') {\n

                $clientsData = $clients ? array_map(fn ($c) => $c->toArray(), $clients) : [];\n

                    'companyName'      => $row['companyname'],\n
                    'workfield'        => $row['workfield'],\n
                    'contactFirstname' => $row['contactfirstname'],\n
                    'contactLastname'  => $row['contactlastname'],\n
                    'contactEmail'     => $row['contactemail'],\n
                    'contactPhone'     => $row['contactphone'] ?? null,\n
                ];\n
            }, $rawRows);\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['clients' => $clientsData, 'total' => count($clientsData)]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage());\n
        }\n
    }\n

                // Validation des champs obligatoires\n
                if (empty($inputData['siret'])) {\n

                }\n

                    throw new \Exception('Company name is required');\n
                }\n
\n

                if (14 !== \strlen($inputData['siret']) || !ctype_digit($inputData['siret'])) {\n

                }\n

                // Vérifier si le client existe déjà\n
                $existingClient = $clientRepo->getByAttributes(['siret' => $inputData['siret']], false);\n

                    throw new \Exception('A client with this SIRET number already exists');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Création du client\n
                $client = new Client();\n
                $client->setSiret($inputData['siret']);\n
                $client->setCompanyName($inputData['companyName']);\n
                $client->setWorkfield($inputData['workfield'] ?? null);\n

                $client->setContactLastname($inputData['contactLastname'] ?? null);\n
                $client->setContactEmail($inputData['contactEmail'] ?? null);\n
                $client->setContactPhone($inputData['contactPhone'] ?? null);\n

                // Création de l'adresse si fournie\n
                $addressData = $inputData['address'] ?? null;\n
                $addressArray = null;\n
\n
                if ($addressData && !empty($addressData['streetNumber']) && !empty($addressData['streetName']) && !empty($addressData['postCode']) && !empty($addressData['city'])) {\n
                    $address = new Address();\n
                    $address->setStreetNumber((int) $addressData['streetNumber']);\n
                    $address->setStreetLetter($addressData['streetLetter'] ?? null);\n
                    $address->setStreetName($addressData['streetName']);\n

                    $address->setCity($addressData['city']);\n
                    $address->setCountry($addressData['country'] ?? null);\n

                    $clientSpecificRepo = new ClientRepository();\n
                    $addressId          = $clientSpecificRepo->insertAddress($address);\n

                    if ($addressId !== null) {\n
                        $addressArray        = $address->toArray();\n
                        $addressArray['id']  = $addressId;\n
                        $clientSpecificRepo->linkAddressToClient($inputData['siret'], $addressId);\n
                    }\n
                }\n

                $responseData['address'] = $addressArray;\n

    /**\n
     * API GET /api/clients/search?q=terme\n
     * Recherche dynamique de clients par raison sociale, SIRET ou secteur.\n
     */\n
    final public function sirenLookup(): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Méthode non autorisée', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $q = trim($_GET['q'] ?? '');\n
\n
        if ($q === '' || !ctype_digit($q)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Numéro invalide : seuls les chiffres sont acceptés', 400);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $apiKey = $_ENV['SIREN_API_KEY'] ?? '';\n
\n
        if (strlen($q) <= 9) {\n
            $url = "https://data.siren-api.fr/v3/unites_legales/{$q}";\n
        } else {\n
            $url = "https://data.siren-api.fr/v3/etablissements/{$q}";\n
        }\n
\n
        $context = stream_context_create([\n
            'http' => [\n
                'method'        => 'GET',\n
                'header'        => "X-Client-Secret: {$apiKey}\r\nAccept: application/json\r\n",\n
                'ignore_errors' => true,\n
                'timeout'       => 10,\n
            ],\n
        ]);\n
\n
        $response = @file_get_contents($url, false, $context);\n
\n
        $httpCode = 200;\n
        if (isset($http_response_header)) {\n
            foreach ($http_response_header as $header) {\n
                if (preg_match('/HTTP\/\S+ (\d+)/', $header, $matches)) {\n
                    $httpCode = (int) $matches[1];\n
                }\n
            }\n
        }\n
\n
        if ($response === false || $httpCode === 503) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Impossible de contacter l\'API SIREN', 503);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if ($httpCode === 404) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Entreprise non trouvée', 404);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $data = json_decode($response, true);\n
\n
        if ($httpCode !== 200 || !$data) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Erreur lors de la récupération des données', 500);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $normalized = [];\n
\n
        if (isset($data['unite_legale'])) {\n
            $ul = $data['unite_legale'];\n
            $denomination = $ul['denomination'] ?? null;\n
            if (!$denomination && isset($ul['nom'])) {\n
                $denomination = trim(($ul['prenom_usuel'] ?? '') . ' ' . $ul['nom']);\n
            }\n
            $normalized['companyName'] = $denomination;\n
            $normalized['workfield']   = $ul['activite_principale'] ?? null;\n
\n
            if (isset($ul['etablissement_siege'])) {\n
                $siege = $ul['etablissement_siege'];\n
                $normalized['streetNumber'] = $siege['numero_voie'] ?? null;\n
                $normalized['streetLetter'] = $siege['indice_repetition'] ?? null;\n
                $streetType = $siege['type_voie'] ?? '';\n
                $streetLabel = $siege['libelle_voie'] ?? '';\n
                $normalized['streetName'] = trim($streetType . ' ' . $streetLabel) ?: null;\n
                $normalized['postCode']   = $siege['code_postal'] ?? null;\n
                $normalized['city']       = $siege['libelle_commune'] ?? null;\n
                $normalized['country']    = 'France';\n
            }\n
        } elseif (isset($data['etablissement'])) {\n
            $etab = $data['etablissement'];\n
            $ul   = $etab['unite_legale'] ?? [];\n
            $denomination = $ul['denomination'] ?? ($etab['enseigne_1'] ?? ($etab['denomination_usuelle'] ?? null));\n
            $normalized['companyName']  = $denomination;\n
            $normalized['workfield']    = $etab['activite_principale'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['streetNumber'] = $etab['numero_voie'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['streetLetter'] = $etab['indice_repetition'] ?? null;\n
            $streetType = $etab['type_voie'] ?? '';\n
            $streetLabel = $etab['libelle_voie'] ?? '';\n
            $normalized['streetName'] = trim($streetType . ' ' . $streetLabel) ?: null;\n
            $normalized['postCode']   = $etab['code_postal'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['city']       = $etab['libelle_commune'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['country']    = 'France';\n
        }\n
\n
        $this->jsonSuccess($normalized);\n
    }\n
\n
    final public function searchApiClients(): void\n
    {\n
        try {\n
            $searchTerm = trim($_GET['q'] ?? '');\n
            $clientRepo = new ClientRepository();\n
\n
            if ($searchTerm === '') {\n
                $clients     = $clientRepo->getAll();\n
                $clientsData = $clients ? array_map(fn ($c) => $c->toArray(), $clients) : [];\n
                $this->jsonSuccess(['clients' => $clientsData, 'total' => count($clientsData)]);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $rawRows = $clientRepo->searchByTerm($searchTerm);\n
\n
            $clientsData = array_map(function (array $row) {\n
                return [\n
                    'siret'            => $row['siret'],\n
                    'companyName'      => $row['companyname'],\n
                    'workfield'        => $row['workfield'],\n
                    'contactFirstname' => $row['contactfirstname'],\n
                    'contactLastname'  => $row['contactlastname'],\n
                    'contactEmail'     => $row['contactemail'],\n
                    'contactPhone'     => $row['contactphone'] ?? null,\n
                ];\n
            }, $rawRows);\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['clients' => $clientsData, 'total' => count($clientsData)]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage());\n
        }\n
    }\n

    final public function addApiClient(): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        if ('POST' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                // Récupération des données JSON\n
                $inputData = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true);\n
\n
                if (!$inputData) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('No data received');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validation des champs obligatoires\n
                if (empty($inputData['siret'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('SIRET number is required');\n
                }\n
                if (empty($inputData['companyName'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Company name is required');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validation du format SIRET (14 caractères)\n
                if (14 !== \strlen($inputData['siret']) || !ctype_digit($inputData['siret'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('SIRET number must be exactly 14 digits');\n
                }\n
\n
                $clientRepo = new Repository(Client::class);\n
\n
                // Vérifier si le client existe déjà\n
                $existingClient = $clientRepo->getByAttributes(['siret' => $inputData['siret']], false);\n
                if ($existingClient) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('A client with this SIRET number already exists');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Création du client\n
                $client = new Client();\n
                $client->setSiret($inputData['siret']);\n
                $client->setCompanyName($inputData['companyName']);\n
                $client->setWorkfield($inputData['workfield'] ?? null);\n
                $client->setContactFirstname($inputData['contactFirstname'] ?? null);\n
                $client->setContactLastname($inputData['contactLastname'] ?? null);\n
                $client->setContactEmail($inputData['contactEmail'] ?? null);\n
                $client->setContactPhone($inputData['contactPhone'] ?? null);\n
\n
                $clientRepo->insert($client);\n
\n
                // Création de l'adresse si fournie\n
                $addressData = $inputData['address'] ?? null;\n
                $addressArray = null;\n
\n
                if ($addressData && !empty($addressData['streetNumber']) && !empty($addressData['streetName']) && !empty($addressData['postCode']) && !empty($addressData['city'])) {\n
                    $address = new Address();\n
                    $address->setStreetNumber((int) $addressData['streetNumber']);\n
                    $address->setStreetLetter($addressData['streetLetter'] ?? null);\n
                    $address->setStreetName($addressData['streetName']);\n
                    $address->setPostCode($addressData['postCode']);\n
                    $address->setState($addressData['state'] ?? null);\n
                    $address->setCity($addressData['city']);\n
                    $address->setCountry($addressData['country'] ?? null);\n
\n
                    // Insertion de l'adresse avec récupération de l'UUID généré\n
                    $clientSpecificRepo = new ClientRepository();\n
                    $addressId          = $clientSpecificRepo->insertAddress($address);\n
\n
                    if ($addressId !== null) {\n
                        $addressArray        = $address->toArray();\n
                        $addressArray['id']  = $addressId;\n
                        $clientSpecificRepo->linkAddressToClient($inputData['siret'], $addressId);\n
                    }\n
                }\n
\n
                $responseData = $client->toArray();\n
                $responseData['address'] = $addressArray;\n
\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'success' => true,\n
                    'message' => 'Client created successfully',\n
                    'client' => $responseData,\n
                ]);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n

    final public function editApiClient(string $siret): void\n
    {\n

                    $client->setWorkfield($inputData['workfield']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['contactFirstname'])) {\n

                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['contactLastname'])) {\n

                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['contactEmail'])) {\n

                if (isset($inputData['contactPhone'])) {\n

                }\n
\n
                // Sauvegarde client avec requête personnalisée car la clé primaire est siret (string)\n
                $clientSpecificRepo = new ClientRepository();\n
                $clientSpecificRepo->updateBySiret($client, $siret);\n

                        'streetletter' => $addressData['streetLetter'] ?? null,\n
                        'streetname'   => $addressData['streetName'],\n
                        'postcode'     => $addressData['postCode'],\n
                        'state'        => $addressData['state'] ?? null,\n
                        'city'         => $addressData['city'],\n
                        'country'      => $addressData['country'] ?? null,\n

\n

                        // Mise à jour de l'adresse existante\n

                            'streetLetter' => $addressData['streetLetter'] ?? null,\n
                            'streetName'   => $addressData['streetName'],\n

    /**\n
     * API GET /api/clients/search?q=terme\n
     * Recherche dynamique de clients par raison sociale, SIRET ou secteur.\n
     */\n
    final public function sirenLookup(): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Méthode non autorisée', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $q = trim($_GET['q'] ?? '');\n
\n
        if ($q === '' || !ctype_digit($q)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Numéro invalide : seuls les chiffres sont acceptés', 400);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $apiKey = $_ENV['SIREN_API_KEY'] ?? '';\n
\n
        if (strlen($q) <= 9) {\n
            $url = "https://data.siren-api.fr/v3/unites_legales/{$q}";\n
        } else {\n
            $url = "https://data.siren-api.fr/v3/etablissements/{$q}";\n
        }\n
\n
        $context = stream_context_create([\n
            'http' => [\n
                'method'        => 'GET',\n
                'header'        => "X-Client-Secret: {$apiKey}\r\nAccept: application/json\r\n",\n
                'ignore_errors' => true,\n
                'timeout'       => 10,\n
            ],\n
        ]);\n
\n
        $response = @file_get_contents($url, false, $context);\n
\n
        $httpCode = 200;\n
        if (isset($http_response_header)) {\n
            foreach ($http_response_header as $header) {\n
                if (preg_match('/HTTP\/\S+ (\d+)/', $header, $matches)) {\n
                    $httpCode = (int) $matches[1];\n
                }\n
            }\n
        }\n
\n
        if ($response === false || $httpCode === 503) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Impossible de contacter l\'API SIREN', 503);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if ($httpCode === 404) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Entreprise non trouvée', 404);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $data = json_decode($response, true);\n
\n
        if ($httpCode !== 200 || !$data) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Erreur lors de la récupération des données', 500);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $normalized = [];\n
\n
        if (isset($data['unite_legale'])) {\n
            $ul = $data['unite_legale'];\n
            $denomination = $ul['denomination'] ?? null;\n
            if (!$denomination && isset($ul['nom'])) {\n
                $denomination = trim(($ul['prenom_usuel'] ?? '') . ' ' . $ul['nom']);\n
            }\n
            $normalized['companyName'] = $denomination;\n
            $normalized['workfield']   = $ul['activite_principale'] ?? null;\n
\n
            if (isset($ul['etablissement_siege'])) {\n
                $siege = $ul['etablissement_siege'];\n
                $normalized['streetNumber'] = $siege['numero_voie'] ?? null;\n
                $normalized['streetLetter'] = $siege['indice_repetition'] ?? null;\n
                $streetType = $siege['type_voie'] ?? '';\n
                $streetLabel = $siege['libelle_voie'] ?? '';\n
                $normalized['streetName'] = trim($streetType . ' ' . $streetLabel) ?: null;\n
                $normalized['postCode']   = $siege['code_postal'] ?? null;\n
                $normalized['city']       = $siege['libelle_commune'] ?? null;\n
                $normalized['country']    = 'France';\n
            }\n
        } elseif (isset($data['etablissement'])) {\n
            $etab = $data['etablissement'];\n
            $ul   = $etab['unite_legale'] ?? [];\n
            $denomination = $ul['denomination'] ?? ($etab['enseigne_1'] ?? ($etab['denomination_usuelle'] ?? null));\n
            $normalized['companyName']  = $denomination;\n
            $normalized['workfield']    = $etab['activite_principale'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['streetNumber'] = $etab['numero_voie'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['streetLetter'] = $etab['indice_repetition'] ?? null;\n
            $streetType = $etab['type_voie'] ?? '';\n
            $streetLabel = $etab['libelle_voie'] ?? '';\n
            $normalized['streetName'] = trim($streetType . ' ' . $streetLabel) ?: null;\n
            $normalized['postCode']   = $etab['code_postal'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['city']       = $etab['libelle_commune'] ?? null;\n
            $normalized['country']    = 'France';\n
        }\n
\n
        $this->jsonSuccess($normalized);\n
    }\n
\n
    final public function searchApiClients(): void\n
    {\n
        try {\n
            $searchTerm = trim($_GET['q'] ?? '');\n
            $clientRepo = new ClientRepository();\n
\n
            if ($searchTerm === '') {\n
                $clients     = $clientRepo->getAll();\n
                $clientsData = $clients ? array_map(fn ($c) => $c->toArray(), $clients) : [];\n
                $this->jsonSuccess(['clients' => $clientsData, 'total' => count($clientsData)]);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $rawRows = $clientRepo->searchByTerm($searchTerm);\n
\n
            $clientsData = array_map(function (array $row) {\n
                return [\n
                    'siret'            => $row['siret'],\n
                    'companyName'      => $row['companyname'],\n
                    'workfield'        => $row['workfield'],\n
                    'contactFirstname' => $row['contactfirstname'],\n
                    'contactLastname'  => $row['contactlastname'],\n
                    'contactEmail'     => $row['contactemail'],\n
                    'contactPhone'     => $row['contactphone'] ?? null,\n
                ];\n
            }, $rawRows);\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['clients' => $clientsData, 'total' => count($clientsData)]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage());\n
        }\n
    }\n

            $stateId = $project['state_id'] ?? null;\n
            if ($stateId && isset($statesById[$stateId])) {\n
                $stateName = strtolower($statesById[$stateId]->getName());\n
                if (str_contains($stateName, 'annul')) {\n
                    ++$statusStats['annule'];\n
                } elseif (str_contains($stateName, 'retard')) {\n
                    ++$statusStats['retarde'];\n
                } elseif (str_contains($stateName, 'termin') || str_contains($stateName, 'done') || str_contains($stateName, 'fini')) {\n
                    ++$statusStats['termine'];\n
                } elseif (str_contains($stateName, 'cours') || str_contains($stateName, 'progress')) {\n
                    ++$statusStats['en_cours'];\n
                } else {\n
                    ++$statusStats['en_attente'];\n
                }\n
            } else {\n
                ++$statusStats['en_attente'];\n
            }\n
        }\n
\n
        $this->render('project/project.php', [\n
            'pageTitle'         => 'Projets',\n
            'projects'          => $projects,\n
            'userRole'          => $userRole,\n
            'statusStats'       => $statusStats,\n
            'states'            => $statesById,\n
            'stateCounts'       => $stateCounts,\n
            'upcomingDeadlines' => $upcomingDeadlines,\n
        ]);\n
    }\n
\n
    // Affichage des détails d'un projet\n
    #[OA\Get(\n
        path: '/project/{id}',\n
        summary: 'Show project details page',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'id', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n
        ],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'Project details page'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 302, description: 'Redirect to projects list if not found'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function show(string $id): void\n
    {\n
        if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($id)) {\n
            header('Location: /projects');\n
            exit;\n
        }\n
\n
        $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
        $userRole    = $currentUser ? ($currentUser->getRoleName() ?? 'USER') : 'USER';\n
        $canCreate   = in_array($userRole, ['ADMIN', 'CDP', 'PDG'], true);\n
        $canDelete   = in_array($userRole, ['ADMIN', 'PDG'], true);\n
\n
        $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
        $userRepo    = new Repository(\Kentec\App\Model\User::class);\n
        $taskRepo    = new TaskRepository();\n
        $stateRepo   = new Repository(State::class);\n
\n
        // Récupérer le projet actif\n
        $project = $projectRepo->findActiveById($id);\n
\n
        if ($project === null) {\n
            header('Location: /projects');\n
            exit;\n
        }\n
\n
        // Contrôle d'accès : USER ne peut voir que les projets sur lesquels il a une tâche\n
        if ($userRole === 'USER' && $currentUser) {\n
            if (!$taskRepo->isUserAssignedToProject($id, $currentUser->getId())) {\n
                header('Location: /projects');\n
                exit;\n
            }\n
        }\n
\n
        // Normalisation des clés\n
        $project['beginDate'] = $project['beginDate'] ?? $project['begindate'] ?? null;\n
        $project['theoricalDeadLine'] = $project['theoricalDeadLine'] ?? $project['theoricaldeadline'] ?? null;\n
        $project['realDeadLine'] = $project['realDeadLine'] ?? $project['realdeadline'] ?? null;\n
\n
        // Récupérer les utilisateurs\n
        $users = $userRepo->getAll();\n
        $usersById = [];\n
        foreach ($users as $user) {\n
            $usersById[$user->getId()] = $user;\n
        }\n
\n
        // Récupérer les états\n
        $states = $stateRepo->getAll();\n
        $statesById = [];\n
        $completedStateId = null;\n
        if ($states) {\n
            foreach ($states as $state) {\n
                $statesById[$state->getId()] = $state;\n
                if (false !== stripos($state->getName(), 'termin')\n
                    || false !== stripos($state->getName(), 'done')\n
                    || false !== stripos($state->getName(), 'clos')\n
                    || false !== stripos($state->getName(), 'fini')) {\n
                    $completedStateId = $state->getId();\n
                }\n
            }\n
        }\n
\n
        // Hydratation manager\n
        if (!empty($project['project_manager_id']) && isset($usersById[$project['project_manager_id']])) {\n
            $project['manager_object'] = $usersById[$project['project_manager_id']];\n
        }\n
\n
        // Récupérer les tâches du projet\n
        $tasks = $taskRepo->getByAttributes(['project_id' => $id]);\n
        if (!is_array($tasks)) {\n
            $tasks = $tasks ? [$tasks] : [];\n
        }\n
\n
        // Récupérer les assignations task->user via la table de liaison\n
        $assignments    = $taskRepo->findAllUserAssignments();\n
        $taskDevelopers = [];\n
        foreach ($assignments as $assignment) {\n
            $taskDevelopers[$assignment['task_id']] = $assignment['user_id'];\n
        }\n
\n
        // Calculs Statistiques\n
        $stats = [\n
            'total' => count($tasks),\n
            'completed' => 0,\n
            'in_progress' => 0,\n
            'todo' => 0,\n
            'progress' => 0,\n
        ];\n
\n
        $absenceRepo   = new AbsenceRepository();\n
        $absenceRows   = $absenceRepo->findActiveTodayWithDates();\n
        $absentUserIds = array_column($absenceRows, 'user_id');\n
        $absenceByUser = [];\n
        foreach ($absenceRows as $row) {\n
            $absenceByUser[$row['user_id']] = $row;\n
        }\n
\n
        $team = [];\n
        // Ajouter le manager à l'équipe\n
        if (!empty($project['project_manager_id']) && isset($usersById[$project['project_manager_id']])) {\n
            $userId = $project['project_manager_id'];\n
            $team[$userId] = [\n
                'user'         => $usersById[$userId],\n
                'role'         => 'Chef de projet',\n
                'active_tasks' => 0,\n
                'is_absent'    => in_array($userId, $absentUserIds, true),\n
                'absence'      => $absenceByUser[$userId] ?? null,\n
            ];\n
        }\n
\n
        foreach ($tasks as $task) {\n
            $stateId = $task->getStateId();\n
\n
            // Stats par état\n
            $stateName = isset($statesById[$stateId]) ? $statesById[$stateId]->getName() : '';\n
\n
            if ($stateId == $completedStateId) {\n
                ++$stats['completed'];\n
            } elseif (false !== stripos($stateName, 'todo')\n
                      || false !== stripos($stateName, 'faire')\n
                      || false !== stripos($stateName, 'attente')\n
                      || false !== stripos($stateName, 'backlog')) {\n
                ++$stats['todo'];\n
            } else {\n
                ++$stats['in_progress'];\n
            }\n
\n
            // Membres de l'équipe via usertaskREL\n
            $devId = $taskDevelopers[$task->getId()] ?? null;\n
            if ($devId && isset($usersById[$devId])) {\n
                if (!isset($team[$devId])) {\n
                    $team[$devId] = [\n
                        'user'         => $usersById[$devId],\n
                        'role'         => 'Développeur',\n
                        'active_tasks' => 0,\n
                        'is_absent'    => in_array($devId, $absentUserIds, true),\n
                        'absence'      => $absenceByUser[$devId] ?? null,\n
                    ];\n
                }\n
                $isCompleted = (false !== stripos($stateName, 'termin')\n
                                || false !== stripos($stateName, 'done')\n
                                || false !== stripos($stateName, 'clos')\n
                                || false !== stripos($stateName, 'fini'));\n
                if (!$isCompleted) {\n
                    ++$team[$devId]['active_tasks'];\n
                }\n
            }\n
        }\n
\n
        $stats['progress'] = $stats['total'] > 0 ? round(($stats['completed'] / $stats['total']) * 100) : 0;\n
\n
        // Effort totals\n
        $effortRequired = 0.0;\n
        $effortMade     = 0.0;\n
        foreach ($tasks as $task) {\n
            $effortRequired += (float) ($task->getEffortrequired() ?? 0);\n
            $effortMade     += (float) ($task->getEffortmade()     ?? 0);\n
        }\n
        $stats['effort_required'] = round($effortRequired, 2);\n
        $stats['effort_made']     = round($effortMade, 2);\n
\n
        $this->render('project/details.php', [\n
            'project'        => $project,\n
            'tasks'          => $tasks,\n
            'stats'          => $stats,\n
            'team'           => $team,\n
            'states'         => $statesById,\n
            'taskDevelopers' => $taskDevelopers,\n
            'userRole'       => $userRole,\n
            'canCreate'      => $canCreate,\n
            'canDelete'      => $canDelete,\n
            'allUsers'       => array_values($usersById),\n
        ]);\n
    }\n
\n
    // API - Récupérer les projets en JSON\n
    #[OA\Get(\n
        path: '/api/projects',\n
        summary: 'Get all projects (JSON)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(\n
                response: 200,\n
                description: 'Successful response',\n
                content: new OA\JsonContent(\n
                    properties: [\n
                        new OA\Property(property: 'projects', type: 'array', items: new OA\Items(ref: '#/components/schemas/Project')),\n
                    ]\n
                )\n
            ),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function getApiProjects(): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être GET', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
            $userRepo    = new Repository(\Kentec\App\Model\User::class);\n
\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
            $userRole    = $currentUser ? ($currentUser->getRoleName() ?? 'USER') : 'USER';\n
\n
            // USER : seulement les projets où il a au moins une tâche assignée\n
            if ($userRole === 'USER' && $currentUser) {\n
                $projects = $projectRepo->findActiveByUserId($currentUser->getId());\n
            } else {\n
                $projects = $projectRepo->findAllActive();\n
            }\n
\n
            $users = $userRepo->getAll();\n
            $usersById = [];\n
            foreach ($users as $user) {\n
                $usersById[$user->getId()] = $user;\n
            }\n
\n
            foreach ($projects as &$project) {\n
                // Normalisation des clés\n
                $project['beginDate'] = $project['beginDate'] ?? $project['begindate'] ?? null;\n
                $project['theoricalDeadLine'] = $project['theoricalDeadLine'] ?? $project['theoricaldeadline'] ?? null;\n
                $project['realDeadLine'] = $project['realDeadLine'] ?? $project['realdeadline'] ?? null;\n
\n
                if (!empty($project['project_manager_id']) && isset($usersById[$project['project_manager_id']])) {\n
                    $manager = $usersById[$project['project_manager_id']];\n
                    $project['manager_firstname'] = $manager->getFirstname();\n
                    $project['manager_lastname'] = $manager->getLastname();\n
                    $project['manager_email'] = $manager->getEmail();\n
                }\n
            }\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['projects' => $projects ?? []]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n
\n
    #[OA\Get(\n
        path: '/api/project/{projectId}',\n
        summary: 'Get project by ID (JSON)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'projectId', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n
        ],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(\n
                response: 200,\n
                description: 'Successful response',\n
                content: new OA\JsonContent(\n
                    properties: [\n
                        new OA\Property(property: 'project', ref: '#/components/schemas/Project'),\n
                    ]\n
                )\n
            ),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 404, description: 'Project not found'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function getApiProject(string $projectId): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être GET', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($projectId)) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Invalid UUID format', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $taskRepo    = new TaskRepository();\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
\n
            // USER : vérifier qu'il a au moins une tâche sur ce projet\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
            $userRole    = $currentUser ? ($currentUser->getRoleName() ?? 'USER') : 'USER';\n
\n
            if ($userRole === 'USER' && $currentUser) {\n
                if (!$taskRepo->isUserAssignedToProject($projectId, $currentUser->getId())) {\n
                    $this->jsonError('Accès non autorisé', 403);\n
                    return;\n
                }\n
            }\n
\n
            $row = $projectRepo->findWithDetailsById($projectId);\n
\n
            if ($row === null) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Projet introuvable', 404);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $project = Project::fromDatabaseArray($row);\n
\n
            // Calcul d'effort via méthode dédiée\n
            $effort = $this->calculerEffortProjet($taskRepo, $projectId);\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess([\n
                'project'            => $project,\n
                'totalEffortRequired' => $effort['totalEffortRequired'],\n
                'totalEffortMade'     => $effort['totalEffortMade'],\n
                'totalTasks'          => $effort['totalTasks'],\n
            ]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n
\n
    /**\n
     * Calcule les totaux d'effort pour un projet.\n
     * Utilise COALESCE pour retourner 0 si aucune tâche n'est associée.\n
     */\n
    private function calculerEffortProjet(TaskRepository $taskRepo, string $projectId): array\n
    {\n
        return $taskRepo->findEffortByProjectId($projectId);\n
    }\n
\n
    final public function dynamicalProjects(): void\n
    {\n
        $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
        $projects    = $projectRepo->findAllActive();\n
        $this->render('project/dynamicalProjects.php', ['projects' => $projects]);\n
    }\n
\n
    #[OA\Delete(\n
        path: '/api/delete/project/{projectId}',\n
        summary: 'Soft-delete project (isactive = false)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'projectId', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n
        ],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'Project soft-deleted'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 404, description: 'Project not found'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function deleteApiProject(string $projectId): void\n
    {\n
        $token = $_SERVER['HTTP_X_CSRF_TOKEN'] ?? '';\n
        if (!Security::verifyCsrfToken($token)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Requête invalide (token CSRF manquant ou expiré).', 403);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if ('DELETE' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être DELETE', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($projectId)) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Invalid Project ID (must be a valid UUID)', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
            $project     = $projectRepo->getById($projectId);\n
\n
            if (!$project) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Project not found', 404);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            // Soft delete : isactive = false (jamais de DELETE physique)\n
            $projectRepo->softDelete($projectId, $currentUser?->getId());\n
\n
            // Archiver également toutes les tâches associées au projet\n
            $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
            $taskRepo->archiveByProject($projectId, $currentUser?->getId());\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Projet et ses tâches archivés avec succès']);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n
\n
    #[OA\Post(\n
        path: '/api/add/project',\n
        summary: 'Add new project (JSON)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        requestBody: new OA\RequestBody(\n
            required: true,\n
            content: new OA\JsonContent(\n
                required: ['name', 'beginDate', 'theoreticalDeadline'],\n
                properties: [\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'name', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'description', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'clientId', type: 'string', format: 'uuid'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'projectManagerId', type: 'string', format: 'uuid'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'beginDate', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'theoreticalDeadline', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'realDeadline', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                ]\n
            )\n
        ),\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'Project created'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 400, description: 'Invalid input'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function addApiProject(): void\n
    {\n
        $token = $_SERVER['HTTP_X_CSRF_TOKEN'] ?? '';\n
        if (!Security::verifyCsrfToken($token)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Requête invalide (token CSRF manquant ou expiré).', 403);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if ('POST' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être POST', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            $inputData = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true);\n
\n
            if (!$inputData) {\n
                $this->jsonError('No data received', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            if (empty($inputData['name'])) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Le nom du projet est obligatoire', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            if (empty($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                $this->jsonError('La date de début est obligatoire', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            if (empty($inputData['theoreticalDeadline'])) {\n
                $this->jsonError("L'échéance théorique est obligatoire.", 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
            $stateRepo   = new Repository(State::class);\n
\n
            $project = new Project();\n
            $project->setName($inputData['name']);\n
            $project->setDescription($inputData['description'] ?? null);\n
            $project->setClientId($inputData['clientId'] ?? null);\n
\n
            // Attribution automatique du chef de projet (utilisateur connecté si non fourni)\n
            $managerId = $inputData['projectManagerId'] ?? null;\n
            if (empty($managerId) && $currentUser) {\n
                $managerId = $currentUser->getId();\n
            }\n
            $project->setProjectManagerId($managerId);\n
\n
            $project->setBeginDate(new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']));\n
            $project->setTheoreticalDeadline(new \DateTime($inputData['theoreticalDeadline']));\n
\n
            if (!empty($inputData['realDeadline'])) {\n
                $project->setRealDeadline(new \DateTime($inputData['realDeadline']));\n
            }\n
\n
            // Attribution automatique du statut "En attente"\n
            $defaultStateId = $projectRepo->findDefaultStateId();\n
            if ($defaultStateId !== null) {\n
                $project->setStateId($defaultStateId);\n
            }\n
\n
            // Champs d'audit\n
            if ($currentUser) {\n
                $project->setCreatedby($currentUser->getId());\n
                $project->setUpdatedby($currentUser->getId());\n
            }\n
\n
            $projectRepo->insert($project);\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['project' => $project->toArray()]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n
\n
    #[OA\Put(\n
        path: '/api/edit/project/{projectId}',\n
        summary: 'Edit project (JSON)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'projectId', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n
        ],\n
        requestBody: new OA\RequestBody(\n
            required: true,\n
            content: new OA\JsonContent(\n
                properties: [\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'name', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'description', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'clientId', type: 'string', format: 'uuid'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'projectManagerId', type: 'string', format: 'uuid'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'stateId', type: 'string', format: 'uuid'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'beginDate', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'theoreticalDeadline', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'realDeadline', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                ]\n
            )\n
        ),\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'Project updated'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 404, description: 'Project not found'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function editApiProject(string $projectId): void\n
    {\n
        $token = $_SERVER['HTTP_X_CSRF_TOKEN'] ?? '';\n
        if (!Security::verifyCsrfToken($token)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Requête invalide (token CSRF manquant ou expiré).', 403);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if ('PUT' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être PUT', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($projectId)) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Invalid UUID format', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $inputData = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true);\n
\n
            if (!$inputData) {\n
                $this->jsonError('No data received', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
            $stateRepo   = new Repository(State::class);\n
            $taskRepo    = new TaskRepository();\n
\n
            $project = $projectRepo->getById($projectId);\n
\n
            if (!$project) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Project not found', 404);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $previousStateId = $project->getStateId();\n
\n
            if (isset($inputData['name'])) {\n
                $project->setName($inputData['name']);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['description'])) {\n
                $project->setDescription($inputData['description']);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['clientId'])) {\n
                $project->setClientId($inputData['clientId']);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['projectManagerId'])) {\n
                $project->setProjectManagerId($inputData['projectManagerId']);\n
            }\n
\n
            // Validation du stateId si fourni\n
            if (isset($inputData['stateId']) && $inputData['stateId'] !== null) {\n
                $stateExists = $stateRepo->getById($inputData['stateId']);\n
                if (!$stateExists) {\n
                    $this->jsonError('Statut invalide : cet identifiant ne correspond à aucun statut existant.', 400);\n
                    return;\n
                }\n
                $project->setStateId($inputData['stateId']);\n
            }\n
\n
            if (isset($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                $project->setBeginDate($inputData['beginDate'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']) : null);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['theoreticalDeadline'])) {\n
                $project->setTheoreticalDeadline($inputData['theoreticalDeadline'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['theoreticalDeadline']) : null);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['realDeadline'])) {\n
                $project->setRealDeadline($inputData['realDeadline'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['realDeadline']) : null);\n
            }\n
\n
            // Champs d'audit\n
            if ($currentUser) {\n
                $project->setUpdatedby($currentUser->getId());\n
            }\n
\n
            // Mise à jour en base avec updatedat = NOW()\n
            $projectRepo->updateProject($project, $projectId);\n

                $newState = $stateRepo->getById($newStateId);\n
                $isLate   = $newState && stripos($newState->getName(), 'retard') !== false;\n
\n
                if (!$isLate) {\n
                    $taskRepo->updateStateForProject($newStateId, $projectId);\n
                }\n
            }\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['project' => $project->toArray()]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n

    #[OA\Get(\n
        path: '/api/project/{projectId}',\n
        summary: 'Get project by ID (JSON)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'projectId', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n

                description: 'Successful response',\n

                        new OA\Property(property: 'project', ref: '#/components/schemas/Project'),\n
                    ]\n
                )\n
            ),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 404, description: 'Project not found'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function getApiProject(string $projectId): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être GET', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($projectId)) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Invalid UUID format', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $taskRepo    = new TaskRepository();\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
\n
            // USER : vérifier qu'il a au moins une tâche sur ce projet\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
            $userRole    = $currentUser ? ($currentUser->getRoleName() ?? 'USER') : 'USER';\n
\n
            if ($userRole === 'USER' && $currentUser) {\n
                if (!$taskRepo->isUserAssignedToProject($projectId, $currentUser->getId())) {\n
                    $this->jsonError('Accès non autorisé', 403);\n
                    return;\n
                }\n
            }\n
\n
            $row = $projectRepo->findWithDetailsById($projectId);\n
\n
            if ($row === null) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Projet introuvable', 404);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $project = Project::fromDatabaseArray($row);\n
\n
            // Calcul d'effort via méthode dédiée\n
            $effort = $this->calculerEffortProjet($taskRepo, $projectId);\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess([\n
                'project'            => $project,\n
                'totalEffortRequired' => $effort['totalEffortRequired'],\n
                'totalEffortMade'     => $effort['totalEffortMade'],\n
                'totalTasks'          => $effort['totalTasks'],\n
            ]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n
\n
    /**\n
     * Calcule les totaux d'effort pour un projet.\n
     * Utilise COALESCE pour retourner 0 si aucune tâche n'est associée.\n
     */\n
    private function calculerEffortProjet(TaskRepository $taskRepo, string $projectId): array\n
    {\n
        return $taskRepo->findEffortByProjectId($projectId);\n
    }\n

    #[OA\Delete(\n
        path: '/api/delete/project/{projectId}',\n
        summary: 'Soft-delete project (isactive = false)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'projectId', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n
        ],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'Project soft-deleted'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 404, description: 'Project not found'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function deleteApiProject(string $projectId): void\n
    {\n
        $token = $_SERVER['HTTP_X_CSRF_TOKEN'] ?? '';\n
        if (!Security::verifyCsrfToken($token)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Requête invalide (token CSRF manquant ou expiré).', 403);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if ('DELETE' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être DELETE', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($projectId)) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Invalid Project ID (must be a valid UUID)', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
            $project     = $projectRepo->getById($projectId);\n
\n
            if (!$project) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Project not found', 404);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            // Soft delete : isactive = false (jamais de DELETE physique)\n
            $projectRepo->softDelete($projectId, $currentUser?->getId());\n
\n
            // Archiver également toutes les tâches associées au projet\n
            $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
            $taskRepo->archiveByProject($projectId, $currentUser?->getId());\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Projet et ses tâches archivés avec succès']);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n

    #[OA\Post(\n
        path: '/api/add/project',\n
        summary: 'Add new project (JSON)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        requestBody: new OA\RequestBody(\n
            required: true,\n
            content: new OA\JsonContent(\n
                required: ['name', 'beginDate', 'theoreticalDeadline'],\n
                properties: [\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'name', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'description', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'clientId', type: 'string', format: 'uuid'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'projectManagerId', type: 'string', format: 'uuid'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'beginDate', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'theoreticalDeadline', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'realDeadline', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                ]\n
            )\n
        ),\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'Project created'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 400, description: 'Invalid input'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function addApiProject(): void\n
    {\n
        $token = $_SERVER['HTTP_X_CSRF_TOKEN'] ?? '';\n
        if (!Security::verifyCsrfToken($token)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Requête invalide (token CSRF manquant ou expiré).', 403);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if ('POST' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être POST', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            $inputData = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true);\n
\n
            if (!$inputData) {\n
                $this->jsonError('No data received', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            if (empty($inputData['name'])) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Le nom du projet est obligatoire', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            if (empty($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                $this->jsonError('La date de début est obligatoire', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            if (empty($inputData['theoreticalDeadline'])) {\n
                $this->jsonError("L'échéance théorique est obligatoire.", 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
            $stateRepo   = new Repository(State::class);\n
\n
            $project = new Project();\n
            $project->setName($inputData['name']);\n
            $project->setDescription($inputData['description'] ?? null);\n
            $project->setClientId($inputData['clientId'] ?? null);\n
\n
            // Attribution automatique du chef de projet (utilisateur connecté si non fourni)\n
            $managerId = $inputData['projectManagerId'] ?? null;\n
            if (empty($managerId) && $currentUser) {\n
                $managerId = $currentUser->getId();\n
            }\n
            $project->setProjectManagerId($managerId);\n
\n
            $project->setBeginDate(new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']));\n
            $project->setTheoreticalDeadline(new \DateTime($inputData['theoreticalDeadline']));\n
\n
            if (!empty($inputData['realDeadline'])) {\n
                $project->setRealDeadline(new \DateTime($inputData['realDeadline']));\n
            }\n
\n
            // Attribution automatique du statut "En attente"\n
            $defaultStateId = $projectRepo->findDefaultStateId();\n
            if ($defaultStateId !== null) {\n
                $project->setStateId($defaultStateId);\n
            }\n
\n
            // Champs d'audit\n
            if ($currentUser) {\n
                $project->setCreatedby($currentUser->getId());\n
                $project->setUpdatedby($currentUser->getId());\n
            }\n
\n
            $projectRepo->insert($project);\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['project' => $project->toArray()]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n
\n
    #[OA\Put(\n
        path: '/api/edit/project/{projectId}',\n
        summary: 'Edit project (JSON)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'projectId', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n

                    new OA\Property(property: 'stateId', type: 'string', format: 'uuid'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'beginDate', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'theoreticalDeadline', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'realDeadline', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                ]\n
            )\n
        ),\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'Project updated'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 404, description: 'Project not found'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function editApiProject(string $projectId): void\n
    {\n
        $token = $_SERVER['HTTP_X_CSRF_TOKEN'] ?? '';\n
        if (!Security::verifyCsrfToken($token)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Requête invalide (token CSRF manquant ou expiré).', 403);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if ('PUT' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être PUT', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($projectId)) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Invalid UUID format', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $inputData = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true);\n
\n
            if (!$inputData) {\n
                $this->jsonError('No data received', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
            $stateRepo   = new Repository(State::class);\n
            $taskRepo    = new TaskRepository();\n
\n
            $project = $projectRepo->getById($projectId);\n
\n
            if (!$project) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Project not found', 404);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $previousStateId = $project->getStateId();\n
\n
            if (isset($inputData['name'])) {\n
                $project->setName($inputData['name']);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['description'])) {\n
                $project->setDescription($inputData['description']);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['clientId'])) {\n
                $project->setClientId($inputData['clientId']);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['projectManagerId'])) {\n
                $project->setProjectManagerId($inputData['projectManagerId']);\n
            }\n
\n
            // Validation du stateId si fourni\n
            if (isset($inputData['stateId']) && $inputData['stateId'] !== null) {\n
                $stateExists = $stateRepo->getById($inputData['stateId']);\n
                if (!$stateExists) {\n
                    $this->jsonError('Statut invalide : cet identifiant ne correspond à aucun statut existant.', 400);\n
                    return;\n
                }\n
                $project->setStateId($inputData['stateId']);\n
            }\n
\n
            if (isset($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                $project->setBeginDate($inputData['beginDate'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']) : null);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['theoreticalDeadline'])) {\n
                $project->setTheoreticalDeadline($inputData['theoreticalDeadline'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['theoreticalDeadline']) : null);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['realDeadline'])) {\n
                $project->setRealDeadline($inputData['realDeadline'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['realDeadline']) : null);\n
            }\n
\n
            // Champs d'audit\n
            if ($currentUser) {\n
                $project->setUpdatedby($currentUser->getId());\n
            }\n
\n
            // Mise à jour en base avec updatedat = NOW()\n
            $projectRepo->updateProject($project, $projectId);\n
\n
            // Mise à jour du statut des tâches (sauf si statut = retardé)\n
            $newStateId = $project->getStateId();\n
            if ($newStateId && $newStateId !== $previousStateId) {\n
                $newState = $stateRepo->getById($newStateId);\n
                $isLate   = $newState && stripos($newState->getName(), 'retard') !== false;\n
\n
                if (!$isLate) {\n
                    $taskRepo->updateStateForProject($newStateId, $projectId);\n
                }\n
            }\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['project' => $project->toArray()]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n
}\n

        $effortMade     = 0.0;\n
        foreach ($tasks as $task) {\n

        }\n
        $stats['effort_required'] = round($effortRequired, 2);\n
        $stats['effort_made']     = round($effortMade, 2);\n

            'project'        => $project,\n
            'tasks'          => $tasks,\n
            'stats'          => $stats,\n
            'team'           => $team,\n
            'states'         => $statesById,\n
            'taskDevelopers' => $taskDevelopers,\n
            'userRole'       => $userRole,\n
            'canCreate'      => $canCreate,\n
            'canDelete'      => $canDelete,\n
            'allUsers'       => array_values($usersById),\n
        ]);\n
    }\n

    // API - Récupérer les projets en JSON\n
    #[OA\Get(\n
        path: '/api/projects',\n

        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(\n
                response: 200,\n

    final public function getApiProjects(): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être GET', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
            $userRepo    = new Repository(\Kentec\App\Model\User::class);\n
\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
            $userRole    = $currentUser ? ($currentUser->getRoleName() ?? 'USER') : 'USER';\n
\n
            // USER : seulement les projets où il a au moins une tâche assignée\n
            if ($userRole === 'USER' && $currentUser) {\n
                $projects = $projectRepo->findActiveByUserId($currentUser->getId());\n
            } else {\n
                $projects = $projectRepo->findAllActive();\n
            }\n

            $usersById = [];\n
            foreach ($users as $user) {\n
                $usersById[$user->getId()] = $user;\n

                // Normalisation des clés\n
                $project['beginDate'] = $project['beginDate'] ?? $project['begindate'] ?? null;\n
                $project['theoricalDeadLine'] = $project['theoricalDeadLine'] ?? $project['theoricaldeadline'] ?? null;\n
                $project['realDeadLine'] = $project['realDeadLine'] ?? $project['realdeadline'] ?? null;\n
\n
                if (!empty($project['project_manager_id']) && isset($usersById[$project['project_manager_id']])) {\n

                    $project['manager_firstname'] = $manager->getFirstname();\n
                    $project['manager_lastname'] = $manager->getLastname();\n
                    $project['manager_email'] = $manager->getEmail();\n
                }\n
            }\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['projects' => $projects ?? []]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
