                ++$statusStats['en_attente'];\n
            }\n
        }\n
\n
        $this->render('project/project.php', [\n
            'pageTitle'         => 'Projets',\n
            'projects'          => $projects,\n
            'userRole'          => $userRole,\n
            'statusStats'       => $statusStats,\n
            'states'            => $statesById,\n
            'stateCounts'       => $stateCounts,\n
            'upcomingDeadlines' => $upcomingDeadlines,\n
        ]);\n
    }\n
\n
    // Affichage des détails d'un projet\n
    #[OA\Get(\n
        path: '/project/{id}',\n
        summary: 'Show project details page',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'id', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n
        ],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'Project details page'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 302, description: 'Redirect to projects list if not found'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function show(string $id): void\n
    {\n
        if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($id)) {\n
            header('Location: /projects');\n
            exit;\n
        }\n
\n
        $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
        $userRole    = $currentUser ? ($currentUser->getRoleName() ?? 'USER') : 'USER';\n
        $canCreate   = in_array($userRole, ['ADMIN', 'CDP', 'PDG'], true);\n
        $canDelete   = in_array($userRole, ['ADMIN', 'PDG'], true);\n
\n
        $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
        $userRepo    = new Repository(\Kentec\App\Model\User::class);\n
        $taskRepo    = new TaskRepository();\n
        $stateRepo   = new Repository(State::class);\n
\n
        // Récupérer le projet actif\n
        $project = $projectRepo->findActiveById($id);\n
\n
        if ($project === null) {\n
            header('Location: /projects');\n
            exit;\n
        }\n
\n
        // Contrôle d'accès : USER ne peut voir que les projets sur lesquels il a une tâche\n
        if ($userRole === 'USER' && $currentUser) {\n
            if (!$taskRepo->isUserAssignedToProject($id, $currentUser->getId())) {\n
                header('Location: /projects');\n
                exit;\n
            }\n
        }\n
\n
        // Normalisation des clés\n
        $project['beginDate'] = $project['beginDate'] ?? $project['begindate'] ?? null;\n
        $project['theoricalDeadLine'] = $project['theoricalDeadLine'] ?? $project['theoricaldeadline'] ?? null;\n
        $project['realDeadLine'] = $project['realDeadLine'] ?? $project['realdeadline'] ?? null;\n
\n
        // Récupérer les utilisateurs\n
        $users = $userRepo->getAll();\n
        $usersById = [];\n
        foreach ($users as $user) {\n
            $usersById[$user->getId()] = $user;\n
        }\n
\n
        // Récupérer les états\n
        $states = $stateRepo->getAll();\n
        $statesById = [];\n
        $completedStateId = null;\n
        if ($states) {\n
            foreach ($states as $state) {\n
                $statesById[$state->getId()] = $state;\n
                if (false !== stripos($state->getName(), 'termin')\n
                    || false !== stripos($state->getName(), 'done')\n
                    || false !== stripos($state->getName(), 'clos')\n
                    || false !== stripos($state->getName(), 'fini')) {\n
                    $completedStateId = $state->getId();\n
                }\n
            }\n
        }\n
\n
        // Hydratation manager\n
        if (!empty($project['project_manager_id']) && isset($usersById[$project['project_manager_id']])) {\n
            $project['manager_object'] = $usersById[$project['project_manager_id']];\n
        }\n
\n
        // Récupérer les tâches du projet\n
        $tasks = $taskRepo->getByAttributes(['project_id' => $id]);\n
        if (!is_array($tasks)) {\n
            $tasks = $tasks ? [$tasks] : [];\n
        }\n
\n
        // Récupérer les assignations task->user via la table de liaison\n
        $assignments    = $taskRepo->findAllUserAssignments();\n
        $taskDevelopers = [];\n
        foreach ($assignments as $assignment) {\n
            $taskDevelopers[$assignment['task_id']] = $assignment['user_id'];\n
        }\n
\n
        // Calculs Statistiques\n
        $stats = [\n
            'total' => count($tasks),\n
            'completed' => 0,\n
            'in_progress' => 0,\n
            'todo' => 0,\n
            'progress' => 0,\n
        ];\n
\n
        $absenceRepo   = new AbsenceRepository();\n
        $absenceRows   = $absenceRepo->findActiveTodayWithDates();\n
        $absentUserIds = array_column($absenceRows, 'user_id');\n
        $absenceByUser = [];\n
        foreach ($absenceRows as $row) {\n
            $absenceByUser[$row['user_id']] = $row;\n
        }\n
\n
        $team = [];\n
        // Ajouter le manager à l'équipe\n
        if (!empty($project['project_manager_id']) && isset($usersById[$project['project_manager_id']])) {\n
            $userId = $project['project_manager_id'];\n
            $team[$userId] = [\n
                'user'         => $usersById[$userId],\n
                'role'         => 'Chef de projet',\n
                'active_tasks' => 0,\n
                'is_absent'    => in_array($userId, $absentUserIds, true),\n
                'absence'      => $absenceByUser[$userId] ?? null,\n
            ];\n
        }\n
\n
        foreach ($tasks as $task) {\n
            $stateId = $task->getStateId();\n
\n
            // Stats par état\n
            $stateName = isset($statesById[$stateId]) ? $statesById[$stateId]->getName() : '';\n
\n
            if ($stateId == $completedStateId) {\n
                ++$stats['completed'];\n
            } elseif (false !== stripos($stateName, 'todo')\n
                      || false !== stripos($stateName, 'faire')\n
                      || false !== stripos($stateName, 'attente')\n
                      || false !== stripos($stateName, 'backlog')) {\n
                ++$stats['todo'];\n
            } else {\n
                ++$stats['in_progress'];\n
            }\n
\n
            // Membres de l'équipe via usertaskREL\n
            $devId = $taskDevelopers[$task->getId()] ?? null;\n
            if ($devId && isset($usersById[$devId])) {\n
                if (!isset($team[$devId])) {\n
                    $team[$devId] = [\n
                        'user'         => $usersById[$devId],\n
                        'role'         => 'Développeur',\n
                        'active_tasks' => 0,\n
                        'is_absent'    => in_array($devId, $absentUserIds, true),\n
                        'absence'      => $absenceByUser[$devId] ?? null,\n
                    ];\n
                }\n
                $isCompleted = (false !== stripos($stateName, 'termin')\n
                                || false !== stripos($stateName, 'done')\n
                                || false !== stripos($stateName, 'clos')\n
                                || false !== stripos($stateName, 'fini'));\n
                if (!$isCompleted) {\n
                    ++$team[$devId]['active_tasks'];\n
                }\n
            }\n
        }\n
\n
        $stats['progress'] = $stats['total'] > 0 ? round(($stats['completed'] / $stats['total']) * 100) : 0;\n
\n
        // Effort totals\n
        $effortRequired = 0.0;\n
        $effortMade     = 0.0;\n
        foreach ($tasks as $task) {\n
            $effortRequired += (float) ($task->getEffortrequired() ?? 0);\n
            $effortMade     += (float) ($task->getEffortmade()     ?? 0);\n
        }\n
        $stats['effort_required'] = round($effortRequired, 2);\n
        $stats['effort_made']     = round($effortMade, 2);\n
\n
        $this->render('project/details.php', [\n
            'project'        => $project,\n
            'tasks'          => $tasks,\n
            'stats'          => $stats,\n
            'team'           => $team,\n
            'states'         => $statesById,\n
            'taskDevelopers' => $taskDevelopers,\n
            'userRole'       => $userRole,\n
            'canCreate'      => $canCreate,\n
            'canDelete'      => $canDelete,\n
            'allUsers'       => array_values($usersById),\n
        ]);\n
    }\n
\n
    // API - Récupérer les projets en JSON\n
    #[OA\Get(\n
        path: '/api/projects',\n
        summary: 'Get all projects (JSON)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(\n
                response: 200,\n
                description: 'Successful response',\n
                content: new OA\JsonContent(\n
                    properties: [\n
                        new OA\Property(property: 'projects', type: 'array', items: new OA\Items(ref: '#/components/schemas/Project')),\n
                    ]\n
                )\n
            ),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function getApiProjects(): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être GET', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
            $userRepo    = new Repository(\Kentec\App\Model\User::class);\n
\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
            $userRole    = $currentUser ? ($currentUser->getRoleName() ?? 'USER') : 'USER';\n
\n
            // USER : seulement les projets où il a au moins une tâche assignée\n
            if ($userRole === 'USER' && $currentUser) {\n
                $projects = $projectRepo->findActiveByUserId($currentUser->getId());\n
            } else {\n
                $projects = $projectRepo->findAllActive();\n
            }\n
\n
            $users = $userRepo->getAll();\n
            $usersById = [];\n
            foreach ($users as $user) {\n
                $usersById[$user->getId()] = $user;\n
            }\n
\n
            foreach ($projects as &$project) {\n
                // Normalisation des clés\n
                $project['beginDate'] = $project['beginDate'] ?? $project['begindate'] ?? null;\n
                $project['theoricalDeadLine'] = $project['theoricalDeadLine'] ?? $project['theoricaldeadline'] ?? null;\n
                $project['realDeadLine'] = $project['realDeadLine'] ?? $project['realdeadline'] ?? null;\n
\n
                if (!empty($project['project_manager_id']) && isset($usersById[$project['project_manager_id']])) {\n
                    $manager = $usersById[$project['project_manager_id']];\n
                    $project['manager_firstname'] = $manager->getFirstname();\n
                    $project['manager_lastname'] = $manager->getLastname();\n
                    $project['manager_email'] = $manager->getEmail();\n
                }\n
            }\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['projects' => $projects ?? []]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n
\n
    #[OA\Get(\n
        path: '/api/project/{projectId}',\n
        summary: 'Get project by ID (JSON)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'projectId', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n
        ],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(\n
                response: 200,\n
                description: 'Successful response',\n
                content: new OA\JsonContent(\n
                    properties: [\n
                        new OA\Property(property: 'project', ref: '#/components/schemas/Project'),\n
                    ]\n
                )\n
            ),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 404, description: 'Project not found'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function getApiProject(string $projectId): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être GET', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($projectId)) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Invalid UUID format', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $taskRepo    = new TaskRepository();\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
\n
            // USER : vérifier qu'il a au moins une tâche sur ce projet\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
            $userRole    = $currentUser ? ($currentUser->getRoleName() ?? 'USER') : 'USER';\n
\n
            if ($userRole === 'USER' && $currentUser) {\n
                if (!$taskRepo->isUserAssignedToProject($projectId, $currentUser->getId())) {\n
                    $this->jsonError('Accès non autorisé', 403);\n
                    return;\n
                }\n
            }\n
\n
            $row = $projectRepo->findWithDetailsById($projectId);\n
\n
            if ($row === null) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Projet introuvable', 404);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $project = Project::fromDatabaseArray($row);\n
\n
            // Calcul d'effort via méthode dédiée\n
            $effort = $this->calculerEffortProjet($taskRepo, $projectId);\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess([\n
                'project'            => $project,\n
                'totalEffortRequired' => $effort['totalEffortRequired'],\n
                'totalEffortMade'     => $effort['totalEffortMade'],\n
                'totalTasks'          => $effort['totalTasks'],\n
            ]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n
\n
    /**\n
     * Calcule les totaux d'effort pour un projet.\n
     * Utilise COALESCE pour retourner 0 si aucune tâche n'est associée.\n
     */\n
    private function calculerEffortProjet(TaskRepository $taskRepo, string $projectId): array\n
    {\n
        return $taskRepo->findEffortByProjectId($projectId);\n
    }\n
\n
    final public function dynamicalProjects(): void\n
    {\n
        $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
        $projects    = $projectRepo->findAllActive();\n
        $this->render('project/dynamicalProjects.php', ['projects' => $projects]);\n
    }\n
\n
    #[OA\Delete(\n
        path: '/api/delete/project/{projectId}',\n
        summary: 'Soft-delete project (isactive = false)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'projectId', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n
        ],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'Project soft-deleted'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 404, description: 'Project not found'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function deleteApiProject(string $projectId): void\n
    {\n
        $token = $_SERVER['HTTP_X_CSRF_TOKEN'] ?? '';\n
        if (!Security::verifyCsrfToken($token)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Requête invalide (token CSRF manquant ou expiré).', 403);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if ('DELETE' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être DELETE', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($projectId)) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Invalid Project ID (must be a valid UUID)', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
            $project     = $projectRepo->getById($projectId);\n
\n
            if (!$project) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Project not found', 404);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            // Soft delete : isactive = false (jamais de DELETE physique)\n
            $projectRepo->softDelete($projectId, $currentUser?->getId());\n
\n
            // Archiver également toutes les tâches associées au projet\n
            $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
            $taskRepo->archiveByProject($projectId, $currentUser?->getId());\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Projet et ses tâches archivés avec succès']);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n
\n
    #[OA\Post(\n
        path: '/api/add/project',\n
        summary: 'Add new project (JSON)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        requestBody: new OA\RequestBody(\n
            required: true,\n
            content: new OA\JsonContent(\n
                required: ['name', 'beginDate', 'theoreticalDeadline'],\n
                properties: [\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'name', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'description', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'clientId', type: 'string', format: 'uuid'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'projectManagerId', type: 'string', format: 'uuid'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'beginDate', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'theoreticalDeadline', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'realDeadline', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                ]\n
            )\n
        ),\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'Project created'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 400, description: 'Invalid input'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function addApiProject(): void\n
    {\n
        $token = $_SERVER['HTTP_X_CSRF_TOKEN'] ?? '';\n
        if (!Security::verifyCsrfToken($token)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Requête invalide (token CSRF manquant ou expiré).', 403);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if ('POST' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être POST', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            $inputData = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true);\n
\n
            if (!$inputData) {\n
                $this->jsonError('No data received', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            if (empty($inputData['name'])) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Le nom du projet est obligatoire', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            if (empty($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                $this->jsonError('La date de début est obligatoire', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            if (empty($inputData['theoreticalDeadline'])) {\n
                $this->jsonError("L'échéance théorique est obligatoire.", 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
            $stateRepo   = new Repository(State::class);\n
\n
            $project = new Project();\n
            $project->setName($inputData['name']);\n
            $project->setDescription($inputData['description'] ?? null);\n
            $project->setClientId($inputData['clientId'] ?? null);\n
\n
            // Attribution automatique du chef de projet (utilisateur connecté si non fourni)\n
            $managerId = $inputData['projectManagerId'] ?? null;\n
            if (empty($managerId) && $currentUser) {\n
                $managerId = $currentUser->getId();\n
            }\n
            $project->setProjectManagerId($managerId);\n
\n
            $project->setBeginDate(new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']));\n
            $project->setTheoreticalDeadline(new \DateTime($inputData['theoreticalDeadline']));\n
\n
            if (!empty($inputData['realDeadline'])) {\n
                $project->setRealDeadline(new \DateTime($inputData['realDeadline']));\n
            }\n
\n
            // Attribution automatique du statut "En attente"\n
            $defaultStateId = $projectRepo->findDefaultStateId();\n
            if ($defaultStateId !== null) {\n
                $project->setStateId($defaultStateId);\n
            }\n
\n
            // Champs d'audit\n
            if ($currentUser) {\n
                $project->setCreatedby($currentUser->getId());\n
                $project->setUpdatedby($currentUser->getId());\n
            }\n
\n
            $projectRepo->insert($project);\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['project' => $project->toArray()]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n
\n
    #[OA\Put(\n
        path: '/api/edit/project/{projectId}',\n
        summary: 'Edit project (JSON)',\n
        tags: ['Projects'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'projectId', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n
        ],\n
        requestBody: new OA\RequestBody(\n
            required: true,\n
            content: new OA\JsonContent(\n
                properties: [\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'name', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'description', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'clientId', type: 'string', format: 'uuid'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'projectManagerId', type: 'string', format: 'uuid'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'stateId', type: 'string', format: 'uuid'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'beginDate', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'theoreticalDeadline', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'realDeadline', type: 'string', format: 'date'),\n
                ]\n
            )\n
        ),\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'Project updated'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 404, description: 'Project not found'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function editApiProject(string $projectId): void\n
    {\n
        $token = $_SERVER['HTTP_X_CSRF_TOKEN'] ?? '';\n
        if (!Security::verifyCsrfToken($token)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Requête invalide (token CSRF manquant ou expiré).', 403);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if ('PUT' !== $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            $this->jsonError('La méthode HTTP doit être PUT', 405);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($projectId)) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Invalid UUID format', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $inputData = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true);\n
\n
            if (!$inputData) {\n
                $this->jsonError('No data received', 400);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
            $stateRepo   = new Repository(State::class);\n
            $taskRepo    = new TaskRepository();\n
\n
            $project = $projectRepo->getById($projectId);\n
\n
            if (!$project) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Project not found', 404);\n
                return;\n
            }\n
\n
            $previousStateId = $project->getStateId();\n
\n
            if (isset($inputData['name'])) {\n
                $project->setName($inputData['name']);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['description'])) {\n
                $project->setDescription($inputData['description']);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['clientId'])) {\n
                $project->setClientId($inputData['clientId']);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['projectManagerId'])) {\n
                $project->setProjectManagerId($inputData['projectManagerId']);\n
            }\n
\n
            // Validation du stateId si fourni\n
            if (isset($inputData['stateId']) && $inputData['stateId'] !== null) {\n
                $stateExists = $stateRepo->getById($inputData['stateId']);\n
                if (!$stateExists) {\n
                    $this->jsonError('Statut invalide : cet identifiant ne correspond à aucun statut existant.', 400);\n
                    return;\n
                }\n
                $project->setStateId($inputData['stateId']);\n
            }\n
\n
            if (isset($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                $project->setBeginDate($inputData['beginDate'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']) : null);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['theoreticalDeadline'])) {\n
                $project->setTheoreticalDeadline($inputData['theoreticalDeadline'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['theoreticalDeadline']) : null);\n
            }\n
            if (isset($inputData['realDeadline'])) {\n
                $project->setRealDeadline($inputData['realDeadline'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['realDeadline']) : null);\n
            }\n
\n
            // Champs d'audit\n
            if ($currentUser) {\n
                $project->setUpdatedby($currentUser->getId());\n
            }\n
\n
            // Mise à jour en base avec updatedat = NOW()\n
            $projectRepo->updateProject($project, $projectId);\n
\n
            // Mise à jour du statut des tâches (sauf si statut = retardé)\n
            $newStateId = $project->getStateId();\n
            if ($newStateId && $newStateId !== $previousStateId) {\n
                $newState = $stateRepo->getById($newStateId);\n
                $isLate   = $newState && stripos($newState->getName(), 'retard') !== false;\n
\n
                if (!$isLate) {\n
                    $taskRepo->updateStateForProject($newStateId, $projectId);\n
                }\n
            }\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['project' => $project->toArray()]);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            $this->jsonError($e->getMessage(), 500);\n
        }\n
    }\n
}\n

    final public function getApiTask(string $taskId): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($taskId)) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Invalid UUID format');\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
\n
                // USER : vérifier qu'il est bien assigné à cette tâche\n
                $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
                $role        = $currentUser ? ($currentUser->getRoleName() ?? 'USER') : 'USER';\n
\n
                if ($role === 'USER' && $currentUser) {\n
                    if (!$taskRepo->isAssignedToUser($taskId, $currentUser->getId())) {\n
                        $this->jsonError('Accès non autorisé', 403);\n
                        return;\n
                    }\n
                }\n
\n
                $task = $taskRepo->getById($taskId);\n
\n
                if (!$task) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('No task found');\n
                }\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'task' => $task->toArray(),\n
                ]);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),\n
                ]);\n
            }\n
        } else {\n
            $this->json([\n
                'success' => false,\n
                'error' => 'La méthode HTTP doit être un GET',\n
            ]);\n
        }\n
    }\n

    final public function deleteApiTask(string $taskId): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        if ('DELETE' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                // Validate taskId\n
                if ('null' === $taskId || '' === $taskId || !InputValidator::validateUuid($taskId)) {\n
                    $this->json([\n
                        'success' => false,\n
                        'error' => 'Invalid task ID',\n
                    ]);\n
\n
                    return;\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
                $task     = $taskRepo->getById($taskId);\n
\n
                if (!$task) {\n
                    $this->json([\n
                        'success' => false,\n
                        'error' => 'Task not found',\n
                    ]);\n
\n
                    return;\n
                }\n
\n
                $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
\n
                // Archiver la tâche (isactive = false) au lieu de la supprimer physiquement\n
                $taskRepo->softDelete($taskId, $currentUser?->getId());\n
\n
                $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Tâche archivée avec succès']);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'success' => false,\n
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),\n
                ]);\n
            }\n
        } else {\n
            $this->json([\n
                'success' => false,\n
                'error' => 'La méthode HTTP doit être DELETE',\n

    final public function addApiTask(): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        if ('POST' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                // Récupération des données JSON\n
                $rawInput = file_get_contents('php://input');\n
                $inputData = json_decode($rawInput, true);\n
\n
                if (!$inputData) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('No data received');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validation des champs obligatoires\n
                if (empty($inputData['name'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Task name is required');\n
                }\n
                if (empty($inputData['type'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Le type de la tâche est obligatoire.');\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
                $task     = new Task();\n
\n
                // Assignation des valeurs\n
                $task->setName($inputData['name']);\n
                $task->setDescription($inputData['description'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setType($inputData['type'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setFormat($inputData['format'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setPriority($inputData['priority'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setDifficulty($inputData['dificulty'] ?? $inputData['difficulty'] ?? null);\n
\n
\n
                // Validate effortRequired\n
                if (!isset($inputData['effortRequired']) || '' === $inputData['effortRequired'] || null === $inputData['effortRequired']) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Le champ effortRequired est obligatoire.');\n
                }\n
                $effort = floatval($inputData['effortRequired']);\n
                if ($effort <= 0 || $effort > 99.99) {\n
                    throw new \Exception("L'effort doit être compris entre 0.01 et 99.99 heures.");\n
                }\n
                $task->setEffortrequired($effort);\n
\n
                // Validate Project ID UUID\n
                if (!empty($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid Project ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setProjectId($inputData['projectId']);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validate State ID UUID\n
                if (!empty($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid State ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setStateId($inputData['stateId']);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Gestion des dates\n
                if (!empty($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setBeginDate(new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']));\n
                }\n
                if (empty($inputData['theoricalEndDate'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception("L'échéance théorique est obligatoire.");\n
                }\n
                $task->setTheoreticalEndDate(new \DateTime($inputData['theoricalEndDate']));\n
                if (!empty($inputData['realEndDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setRealEndDate(new \DateTime($inputData['realEndDate']));\n
                }\n
\n
                // Sauvegarde avec récupération de l'ID généré\n
                $newTaskId = $taskRepo->insertAndReturnId($task);\n
\n
                // Assignation du développeur\n
                if ($newTaskId && !empty($inputData['developerId']) && InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['developerId'])) {\n
                    $taskRepo->deleteUserAssignment($newTaskId);\n
                    $taskRepo->insertUserAssignment($inputData['developerId'], $newTaskId);\n
                }\n
\n
                $this->jsonSuccess([\n
                    'message' => 'Task created successfully',\n
                    'task' => $task->toArray(),\n
                ]);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'success' => false,\n
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),\n
                ]);\n
            }\n
        } else {\n
            $this->json([\n
                'success' => false,\n
                'error' => 'La méthode HTTP doit être POST',\n
            ]);\n
        }\n
    }\n

    final public function editApiTask(string $taskId): void\n
    {\n

                    throw new \Exception('No data received');\n
                }\n

                $task     = $taskRepo->getById($taskId);\n
\n
                if (!$task) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Task not found');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Mise à jour des champs\n
                if (isset($inputData['name'])) {\n
                    $task->setName($inputData['name']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['description'])) {\n
                    $task->setDescription($inputData['description']);\n

                    $task->setType($inputData['type']);\n

                    $task->setFormat($inputData['format']);\n

                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['dificulty'])) {\n
                    $task->setDifficulty($inputData['dificulty'] ?? $inputData['difficulty']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['effortRequired'])) {\n
                    $effort = floatval($inputData['effortRequired']);\n
                    if ($effort <= 0 || $effort > 99.99) {\n
                        throw new \Exception("L'effort doit être compris entre 0.01 et 99.99 heures.");\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setEffortrequired($effort);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['effortMade'])) {\n
                    $effortMade = floatval($inputData['effortMade']);\n
                    if ($effortMade <= 0) {\n
                        throw new \Exception("L'effort réel doit être supérieur à 0.");\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setEffortmade($effortMade);\n
                }\n
                if (!empty($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid Project ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setProjectId($inputData['projectId']);\n
                }\n
                if (!empty($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['stateId'])) {\n

                    }\n
                    $task->setStateId($inputData['stateId']);\n
                }\n

                // Gestion des dates\n
                if (isset($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setBeginDate($inputData['beginDate'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']) : null);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['theoricalEndDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setTheoreticalEndDate($inputData['theoricalEndDate'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['theoricalEndDate']) : null);\n

    final public function getApiTask(string $taskId): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($taskId)) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Invalid UUID format');\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
\n
                // USER : vérifier qu'il est bien assigné à cette tâche\n
                $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
                $role        = $currentUser ? ($currentUser->getRoleName() ?? 'USER') : 'USER';\n
\n
                if ($role === 'USER' && $currentUser) {\n
                    if (!$taskRepo->isAssignedToUser($taskId, $currentUser->getId())) {\n
                        $this->jsonError('Accès non autorisé', 403);\n
                        return;\n
                    }\n
                }\n
\n
                $task = $taskRepo->getById($taskId);\n
\n
                if (!$task) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('No task found');\n
                }\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'task' => $task->toArray(),\n
                ]);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),\n
                ]);\n
            }\n
        } else {\n
            $this->json([\n
                'success' => false,\n
                'error' => 'La méthode HTTP doit être un GET',\n
            ]);\n
        }\n
    }\n

    final public function deleteApiTask(string $taskId): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        if ('DELETE' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                // Validate taskId\n
                if ('null' === $taskId || '' === $taskId || !InputValidator::validateUuid($taskId)) {\n
                    $this->json([\n
                        'success' => false,\n
                        'error' => 'Invalid task ID',\n
                    ]);\n
\n
                    return;\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
                $task     = $taskRepo->getById($taskId);\n
\n
                if (!$task) {\n
                    $this->json([\n
                        'success' => false,\n
                        'error' => 'Task not found',\n
                    ]);\n
\n
                    return;\n
                }\n
\n
                $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
\n
                // Archiver la tâche (isactive = false) au lieu de la supprimer physiquement\n
                $taskRepo->softDelete($taskId, $currentUser?->getId());\n
\n
                $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Tâche archivée avec succès']);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'success' => false,\n

                ]);\n

    final public function addApiTask(): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        if ('POST' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                // Récupération des données JSON\n
                $rawInput = file_get_contents('php://input');\n
                $inputData = json_decode($rawInput, true);\n
\n
                if (!$inputData) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('No data received');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validation des champs obligatoires\n
                if (empty($inputData['name'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Task name is required');\n
                }\n
                if (empty($inputData['type'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Le type de la tâche est obligatoire.');\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
                $task     = new Task();\n
\n
                // Assignation des valeurs\n
                $task->setName($inputData['name']);\n
                $task->setDescription($inputData['description'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setType($inputData['type'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setFormat($inputData['format'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setPriority($inputData['priority'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setDifficulty($inputData['dificulty'] ?? $inputData['difficulty'] ?? null);\n
\n
\n
                // Validate effortRequired\n
                if (!isset($inputData['effortRequired']) || '' === $inputData['effortRequired'] || null === $inputData['effortRequired']) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Le champ effortRequired est obligatoire.');\n
                }\n
                $effort = floatval($inputData['effortRequired']);\n
                if ($effort <= 0 || $effort > 99.99) {\n
                    throw new \Exception("L'effort doit être compris entre 0.01 et 99.99 heures.");\n
                }\n
                $task->setEffortrequired($effort);\n
\n
                // Validate Project ID UUID\n
                if (!empty($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid Project ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setProjectId($inputData['projectId']);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validate State ID UUID\n
                if (!empty($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid State ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setStateId($inputData['stateId']);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Gestion des dates\n
                if (!empty($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setBeginDate(new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']));\n
                }\n
                if (empty($inputData['theoricalEndDate'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception("L'échéance théorique est obligatoire.");\n
                }\n
                $task->setTheoreticalEndDate(new \DateTime($inputData['theoricalEndDate']));\n
                if (!empty($inputData['realEndDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setRealEndDate(new \DateTime($inputData['realEndDate']));\n
                }\n
\n
                // Sauvegarde avec récupération de l'ID généré\n
                $newTaskId = $taskRepo->insertAndReturnId($task);\n
\n
                // Assignation du développeur\n
                if ($newTaskId && !empty($inputData['developerId']) && InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['developerId'])) {\n
                    $taskRepo->deleteUserAssignment($newTaskId);\n
                    $taskRepo->insertUserAssignment($inputData['developerId'], $newTaskId);\n
                }\n
\n
                $this->jsonSuccess([\n
                    'message' => 'Task created successfully',\n
                    'task' => $task->toArray(),\n
                ]);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'success' => false,\n
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),\n
                ]);\n
            }\n
        } else {\n
            $this->json([\n
                'success' => false,\n
                'error' => 'La méthode HTTP doit être POST',\n
            ]);\n
        }\n
    }\n
\n

    final public function getApiTask(string $taskId): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($taskId)) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Invalid UUID format');\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
\n
                // USER : vérifier qu'il est bien assigné à cette tâche\n
                $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
                $role        = $currentUser ? ($currentUser->getRoleName() ?? 'USER') : 'USER';\n
\n
                if ($role === 'USER' && $currentUser) {\n
                    if (!$taskRepo->isAssignedToUser($taskId, $currentUser->getId())) {\n
                        $this->jsonError('Accès non autorisé', 403);\n
                        return;\n
                    }\n
                }\n
\n
                $task = $taskRepo->getById($taskId);\n
\n
                if (!$task) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('No task found');\n
                }\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'task' => $task->toArray(),\n
                ]);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),\n
                ]);\n
            }\n
        } else {\n
            $this->json([\n
                'success' => false,\n
                'error' => 'La méthode HTTP doit être un GET',\n
            ]);\n
        }\n
    }\n

    final public function deleteApiTask(string $taskId): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        if ('DELETE' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                // Validate taskId\n
                if ('null' === $taskId || '' === $taskId || !InputValidator::validateUuid($taskId)) {\n
                    $this->json([\n
                        'success' => false,\n
                        'error' => 'Invalid task ID',\n
                    ]);\n
\n
                    return;\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
                $task     = $taskRepo->getById($taskId);\n
\n
                if (!$task) {\n
                    $this->json([\n
                        'success' => false,\n
                        'error' => 'Task not found',\n
                    ]);\n
\n
                    return;\n
                }\n
\n
                $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
\n
                // Archiver la tâche (isactive = false) au lieu de la supprimer physiquement\n
                $taskRepo->softDelete($taskId, $currentUser?->getId());\n
\n
                $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Tâche archivée avec succès']);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'success' => false,\n

    final public function addApiTask(): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        if ('POST' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                // Récupération des données JSON\n
                $rawInput = file_get_contents('php://input');\n
                $inputData = json_decode($rawInput, true);\n
\n
                if (!$inputData) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('No data received');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validation des champs obligatoires\n
                if (empty($inputData['name'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Task name is required');\n
                }\n
                if (empty($inputData['type'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Le type de la tâche est obligatoire.');\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
                $task     = new Task();\n
\n
                // Assignation des valeurs\n
                $task->setName($inputData['name']);\n
                $task->setDescription($inputData['description'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setType($inputData['type'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setFormat($inputData['format'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setPriority($inputData['priority'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setDifficulty($inputData['dificulty'] ?? $inputData['difficulty'] ?? null);\n
\n
\n
                // Validate effortRequired\n
                if (!isset($inputData['effortRequired']) || '' === $inputData['effortRequired'] || null === $inputData['effortRequired']) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Le champ effortRequired est obligatoire.');\n
                }\n
                $effort = floatval($inputData['effortRequired']);\n
                if ($effort <= 0 || $effort > 99.99) {\n
                    throw new \Exception("L'effort doit être compris entre 0.01 et 99.99 heures.");\n
                }\n
                $task->setEffortrequired($effort);\n
\n
                // Validate Project ID UUID\n
                if (!empty($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid Project ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setProjectId($inputData['projectId']);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validate State ID UUID\n
                if (!empty($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid State ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setStateId($inputData['stateId']);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Gestion des dates\n
                if (!empty($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setBeginDate(new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']));\n
                }\n
                if (empty($inputData['theoricalEndDate'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception("L'échéance théorique est obligatoire.");\n
                }\n
                $task->setTheoreticalEndDate(new \DateTime($inputData['theoricalEndDate']));\n
                if (!empty($inputData['realEndDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setRealEndDate(new \DateTime($inputData['realEndDate']));\n
                }\n
\n
                // Sauvegarde avec récupération de l'ID généré\n
                $newTaskId = $taskRepo->insertAndReturnId($task);\n
\n
                // Assignation du développeur\n
                if ($newTaskId && !empty($inputData['developerId']) && InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['developerId'])) {\n
                    $taskRepo->deleteUserAssignment($newTaskId);\n
                    $taskRepo->insertUserAssignment($inputData['developerId'], $newTaskId);\n
                }\n
\n
                $this->jsonSuccess([\n
                    'message' => 'Task created successfully',\n
                    'task' => $task->toArray(),\n
                ]);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'success' => false,\n
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),\n
                ]);\n
            }\n
        } else {\n
            $this->json([\n
                'success' => false,\n
                'error' => 'La méthode HTTP doit être POST',\n
            ]);\n
        }\n
    }\n
\n

                    $task->setEffortmade($effortMade);\n

    final public function getApiTask(string $taskId): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($taskId)) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Invalid UUID format');\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
\n
                // USER : vérifier qu'il est bien assigné à cette tâche\n
                $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
                $role        = $currentUser ? ($currentUser->getRoleName() ?? 'USER') : 'USER';\n
\n
                if ($role === 'USER' && $currentUser) {\n
                    if (!$taskRepo->isAssignedToUser($taskId, $currentUser->getId())) {\n
                        $this->jsonError('Accès non autorisé', 403);\n
                        return;\n
                    }\n
                }\n
\n
                $task = $taskRepo->getById($taskId);\n
\n
                if (!$task) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('No task found');\n
                }\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'task' => $task->toArray(),\n
                ]);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),\n
                ]);\n
            }\n
        } else {\n
            $this->json([\n
                'success' => false,\n
                'error' => 'La méthode HTTP doit être un GET',\n
            ]);\n
        }\n
    }\n

    final public function addApiTask(): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        if ('POST' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                // Récupération des données JSON\n
                $rawInput = file_get_contents('php://input');\n
                $inputData = json_decode($rawInput, true);\n
\n
                if (!$inputData) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('No data received');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validation des champs obligatoires\n
                if (empty($inputData['name'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Task name is required');\n
                }\n
                if (empty($inputData['type'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Le type de la tâche est obligatoire.');\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
                $task     = new Task();\n
\n
                // Assignation des valeurs\n
                $task->setName($inputData['name']);\n
                $task->setDescription($inputData['description'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setType($inputData['type'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setFormat($inputData['format'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setPriority($inputData['priority'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setDifficulty($inputData['dificulty'] ?? $inputData['difficulty'] ?? null);\n
\n
\n
                // Validate effortRequired\n
                if (!isset($inputData['effortRequired']) || '' === $inputData['effortRequired'] || null === $inputData['effortRequired']) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Le champ effortRequired est obligatoire.');\n
                }\n
                $effort = floatval($inputData['effortRequired']);\n
                if ($effort <= 0 || $effort > 99.99) {\n
                    throw new \Exception("L'effort doit être compris entre 0.01 et 99.99 heures.");\n
                }\n
                $task->setEffortrequired($effort);\n
\n
                // Validate Project ID UUID\n
                if (!empty($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid Project ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setProjectId($inputData['projectId']);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validate State ID UUID\n
                if (!empty($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid State ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setStateId($inputData['stateId']);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Gestion des dates\n
                if (!empty($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setBeginDate(new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']));\n
                }\n
                if (empty($inputData['theoricalEndDate'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception("L'échéance théorique est obligatoire.");\n
                }\n
                $task->setTheoreticalEndDate(new \DateTime($inputData['theoricalEndDate']));\n
                if (!empty($inputData['realEndDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setRealEndDate(new \DateTime($inputData['realEndDate']));\n
                }\n
\n
                // Sauvegarde avec récupération de l'ID généré\n
                $newTaskId = $taskRepo->insertAndReturnId($task);\n
\n
                // Assignation du développeur\n
                if ($newTaskId && !empty($inputData['developerId']) && InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['developerId'])) {\n
                    $taskRepo->deleteUserAssignment($newTaskId);\n
                    $taskRepo->insertUserAssignment($inputData['developerId'], $newTaskId);\n
                }\n
\n
                $this->jsonSuccess([\n
                    'message' => 'Task created successfully',\n
                    'task' => $task->toArray(),\n
                ]);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'success' => false,\n
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),\n
                ]);\n
            }\n
        } else {\n
            $this->json([\n
                'success' => false,\n
                'error' => 'La méthode HTTP doit être POST',\n
            ]);\n
        }\n
    }\n

                    $task->setDifficulty($inputData['dificulty'] ?? $inputData['difficulty']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['effortRequired'])) {\n
                    $effort = floatval($inputData['effortRequired']);\n
                    if ($effort <= 0 || $effort > 99.99) {\n
                        throw new \Exception("L'effort doit être compris entre 0.01 et 99.99 heures.");\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setEffortrequired($effort);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['effortMade'])) {\n
                    $effortMade = floatval($inputData['effortMade']);\n
                    if ($effortMade <= 0) {\n
                        throw new \Exception("L'effort réel doit être supérieur à 0.");\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setEffortmade($effortMade);\n
                }\n
                if (!empty($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid Project ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setProjectId($inputData['projectId']);\n
                }\n
                if (!empty($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid State ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setStateId($inputData['stateId']);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Gestion des dates\n
                if (isset($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setBeginDate($inputData['beginDate'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']) : null);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['theoricalEndDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setTheoreticalEndDate($inputData['theoricalEndDate'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['theoricalEndDate']) : null);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['realEndDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setRealEndDate($inputData['realEndDate'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['realEndDate']) : null);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Sauvegarde\n
                $taskRepo->update($task);\n
\n
                // Assignation du développeur\n
                if (!empty($inputData['developerId']) && InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['developerId'])) {\n
                    $taskRepo->deleteUserAssignment($taskId);\n
                    $taskRepo->insertUserAssignment($inputData['developerId'], $taskId);\n
                }\n
\n
                $this->jsonSuccess([\n
                    'message' => 'Task updated successfully',\n
                    'task' => $task->toArray(),\n
                ]);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'success' => false,\n
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),\n
                ]);\n

                'success' => false,\n
                'error' => 'La méthode HTTP doit être PUT',\n
            ]);\n

    final public function getApiTask(string $taskId): void\n
    {\n
        if ('GET' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($taskId)) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Invalid UUID format');\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
\n
                // USER : vérifier qu'il est bien assigné à cette tâche\n
                $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
                $role        = $currentUser ? ($currentUser->getRoleName() ?? 'USER') : 'USER';\n
\n
                if ($role === 'USER' && $currentUser) {\n
                    if (!$taskRepo->isAssignedToUser($taskId, $currentUser->getId())) {\n
                        $this->jsonError('Accès non autorisé', 403);\n
                        return;\n
                    }\n
                }\n
\n
                $task = $taskRepo->getById($taskId);\n
\n
                if (!$task) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('No task found');\n
                }\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'task' => $task->toArray(),\n
                ]);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),\n
                ]);\n
            }\n
        } else {\n
            $this->json([\n
                'success' => false,\n
                'error' => 'La méthode HTTP doit être un GET',\n
            ]);\n
        }\n
    }\n

    {\n

                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n

                        'error' => 'Task not found',\n
                    ]);\n
\n
                    return;\n

\n
                $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
\n
                // Archiver la tâche (isactive = false) au lieu de la supprimer physiquement\n
                $taskRepo->softDelete($taskId, $currentUser?->getId());\n
\n
                $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Tâche archivée avec succès']);\n

                $this->json([\n

    final public function addApiTask(): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        if ('POST' === $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD']) {\n
            try {\n
                // Récupération des données JSON\n
                $rawInput = file_get_contents('php://input');\n
                $inputData = json_decode($rawInput, true);\n
\n
                if (!$inputData) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('No data received');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validation des champs obligatoires\n
                if (empty($inputData['name'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Task name is required');\n
                }\n
                if (empty($inputData['type'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Le type de la tâche est obligatoire.');\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
                $task     = new Task();\n
\n
                // Assignation des valeurs\n
                $task->setName($inputData['name']);\n
                $task->setDescription($inputData['description'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setType($inputData['type'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setFormat($inputData['format'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setPriority($inputData['priority'] ?? null);\n
                $task->setDifficulty($inputData['dificulty'] ?? $inputData['difficulty'] ?? null);\n
\n
\n
                // Validate effortRequired\n
                if (!isset($inputData['effortRequired']) || '' === $inputData['effortRequired'] || null === $inputData['effortRequired']) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Le champ effortRequired est obligatoire.');\n
                }\n
                $effort = floatval($inputData['effortRequired']);\n
                if ($effort <= 0 || $effort > 99.99) {\n
                    throw new \Exception("L'effort doit être compris entre 0.01 et 99.99 heures.");\n
                }\n
                $task->setEffortrequired($effort);\n
\n
                // Validate Project ID UUID\n
                if (!empty($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid Project ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setProjectId($inputData['projectId']);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Validate State ID UUID\n
                if (!empty($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid State ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setStateId($inputData['stateId']);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Gestion des dates\n
                if (!empty($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setBeginDate(new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']));\n
                }\n
                if (empty($inputData['theoricalEndDate'])) {\n
                    throw new \Exception("L'échéance théorique est obligatoire.");\n
                }\n
                $task->setTheoreticalEndDate(new \DateTime($inputData['theoricalEndDate']));\n
                if (!empty($inputData['realEndDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setRealEndDate(new \DateTime($inputData['realEndDate']));\n
                }\n
\n
                // Sauvegarde avec récupération de l'ID généré\n
                $newTaskId = $taskRepo->insertAndReturnId($task);\n
\n
                // Assignation du développeur\n
                if ($newTaskId && !empty($inputData['developerId']) && InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['developerId'])) {\n
                    $taskRepo->deleteUserAssignment($newTaskId);\n
                    $taskRepo->insertUserAssignment($inputData['developerId'], $newTaskId);\n
                }\n
\n
                $this->jsonSuccess([\n
                    'message' => 'Task created successfully',\n
                    'task' => $task->toArray(),\n
                ]);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'success' => false,\n
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),\n
                ]);\n
            }\n
        } else {\n
            $this->json([\n
                'success' => false,\n
                'error' => 'La méthode HTTP doit être POST',\n
            ]);\n
        }\n
    }\n

                $inputData = json_decode($rawInput, true);\n
\n
                if (!$inputData) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('No data received');\n
                }\n
\n
                $taskRepo = new TaskRepository();\n
                $task     = $taskRepo->getById($taskId);\n
\n
                if (!$task) {\n
                    throw new \Exception('Task not found');\n
                }\n
\n
                // Mise à jour des champs\n
                if (isset($inputData['name'])) {\n
                    $task->setName($inputData['name']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['description'])) {\n
                    $task->setDescription($inputData['description']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['type'])) {\n
                    $task->setType($inputData['type']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['format'])) {\n
                    $task->setFormat($inputData['format']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['priority'])) {\n
                    $task->setPriority($inputData['priority']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['dificulty'])) {\n
                    $task->setDifficulty($inputData['dificulty'] ?? $inputData['difficulty']);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['effortRequired'])) {\n
                    $effort = floatval($inputData['effortRequired']);\n
                    if ($effort <= 0 || $effort > 99.99) {\n
                        throw new \Exception("L'effort doit être compris entre 0.01 et 99.99 heures.");\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setEffortrequired($effort);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['effortMade'])) {\n
                    $effortMade = floatval($inputData['effortMade']);\n
                    if ($effortMade <= 0) {\n
                        throw new \Exception("L'effort réel doit être supérieur à 0.");\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setEffortmade($effortMade);\n
                }\n
                if (!empty($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['projectId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid Project ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setProjectId($inputData['projectId']);\n
                }\n
                if (!empty($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                    if (!InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['stateId'])) {\n
                        throw new \Exception('Invalid State ID (must be a valid UUID)');\n
                    }\n
                    $task->setStateId($inputData['stateId']);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Gestion des dates\n
                if (isset($inputData['beginDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setBeginDate($inputData['beginDate'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['beginDate']) : null);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['theoricalEndDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setTheoreticalEndDate($inputData['theoricalEndDate'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['theoricalEndDate']) : null);\n
                }\n
                if (isset($inputData['realEndDate'])) {\n
                    $task->setRealEndDate($inputData['realEndDate'] ? new \DateTime($inputData['realEndDate']) : null);\n
                }\n
\n
                // Sauvegarde\n
                $taskRepo->update($task);\n
\n
                // Assignation du développeur\n
                if (!empty($inputData['developerId']) && InputValidator::validateUuid($inputData['developerId'])) {\n
                    $taskRepo->deleteUserAssignment($taskId);\n
                    $taskRepo->insertUserAssignment($inputData['developerId'], $taskId);\n
                }\n
\n
                $this->jsonSuccess([\n
                    'message' => 'Task updated successfully',\n
                    'task' => $task->toArray(),\n
                ]);\n
            } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                $this->json([\n
                    'success' => false,\n
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),\n
                ]);\n
            }\n
        } else {\n
            $this->json([\n
                'success' => false,\n
                'error' => 'La méthode HTTP doit être PUT',\n
            ]);\n
        }\n
    }\n

    #[OA\Post(\n

        summary: 'Change current user password',\n

            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'Password changed'),\n

            new OA\Response(response: 401, description: 'Current password incorrect'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function changePassword(): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
        if (!$currentUser) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Non authentifié', 401);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $donnees = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true);\n
\n
        if (empty($donnees['currentPassword']) || empty($donnees['newPassword'])) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Les champs mot de passe actuel et nouveau mot de passe sont obligatoires');\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if (!password_verify($donnees['currentPassword'], $currentUser->getPassword())) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Mot de passe actuel incorrect', 401);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if (strlen($donnees['newPassword']) < 8) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Le nouveau mot de passe doit contenir au moins 8 caractères');\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $userRepo = new Repository(User::class);\n
        $utilisateur = $userRepo->getById($currentUser->getId());\n
\n
        if (!$utilisateur) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Utilisateur introuvable', 404);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $utilisateur->setPassword(password_hash($donnees['newPassword'], PASSWORD_ARGON2I));\n
        $utilisateur->setUpdatedat((new \DateTime())->format('Y-m-d H:i:s'));\n
        $utilisateur->setUpdatedby($currentUser->getId());\n
\n
        $userRepo->update($utilisateur);\n
\n
        $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Mot de passe modifié avec succès']);\n
    }\n

    #[OA\Delete(\n
        path: '/api/delete/user/{userId}',\n
        summary: 'Delete user (soft delete)',\n
        tags: ['Users'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'userId', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n
        ],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'User deactivated'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 403, description: 'Forbidden'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function deleteApiUser(string $userId): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        $adminConnecte = Security::getUser();\n
\n
        // Empêcher l'auto-suppression (utiliser /api/delete/my-account à la place)\n
        if ($adminConnecte !== null && $adminConnecte->getId() === $userId) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Vous ne pouvez pas désactiver votre propre compte via cette route.', 403);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $userRepo = new Repository(User::class);\n
        $utilisateur = $userRepo->getById($userId);\n
\n
        if ($utilisateur === null) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Utilisateur introuvable', 404);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        // Un ADMIN ne peut pas désactiver un PDG\n
        if ($adminConnecte !== null\n
            && $adminConnecte->getRoleName() === 'ADMIN'\n
            && $utilisateur->getRoleName() === 'PDG') {\n
            $this->jsonError('Un administrateur ne peut pas désactiver un PDG.', 403);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        // Soft delete : on désactive sans supprimer physiquement\n
        $utilisateur->setIsactive(false);\n
        //A la place $utilisateurs->delete($utilisateur)\n
        $utilisateur->setUpdatedat((new \DateTime())->format('Y-m-d H:i:s'));\n
\n
        if ($adminConnecte !== null) {\n
            $utilisateur->setUpdatedby($adminConnecte->getId());\n
        }\n
\n
        $userRepo->update($utilisateur);\n
\n
        $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Utilisateur désactivé avec succès']);\n
    }\n

    #[OA\Delete(\n
        path: '/api/delete/my-account',\n
        summary: 'Delete current user account',\n
        tags: ['Users'],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'User account deleted successfully'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 401, description: 'Unauthorized')\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function deleteMyAccount(): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
        if (!$currentUser) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Non authentifié', 401);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            $userId      = $currentUser->getId();\n
            $userRepo    = new UserRepository();\n
            $taskRepo    = new TaskRepository();\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
\n
            $safe = function (callable $fn): void {\n
                try {\n
                    $fn();\n
                } catch (\PDOException $e) {\n
                    $code = $e->getCode();\n
                    if ($code !== '42703' && $code !== '42P01') {\n
                        throw $e;\n
                    }\n
                } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                    if (strpos($e->getMessage(), 'SQLSTATE[42703]') === false && strpos($e->getMessage(), 'SQLSTATE[42P01]') === false) {\n
                        throw $e;\n
                    }\n
                }\n
            };\n
\n
            $safe(fn () => $projectRepo->nullifyManagerReferences($userId));\n
            $safe(fn () => $projectRepo->nullifyUserReferences($userId));\n
            $safe(fn () => $taskRepo->nullifyDeveloperReferences($userId));\n
            $safe(fn () => $taskRepo->deleteAllUserAssignments($userId));\n
            $safe(fn () => $userRepo->deleteAddressReferences($userId));\n
\n
            $userRepo->delete($userId);\n
\n
            Security::disconnect();\n
            setcookie('jwt_token', '', [\n
                'expires'  => time() - 3600,\n
                'path'     => '/',\n
                'httponly' => true,\n
                'secure'   => ($_ENV['APP_ENV'] ?? 'development') === 'production',\n
                'samesite' => 'Lax',\n
            ]);\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Compte supprimé avec succès']);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            error_log('[UsersController::deleteMyAccount] Error: ' . $e->getMessage());\n
            $this->jsonError('Une erreur est survenue lors de la suppression du compte');\n
        }\n
    }\n
}\n

            'pageTitle'        => 'Utilisateurs',\n
            'users'            => $rows,\n
            'userCountByRole'  => $userCountByRole,\n
            'totalActiveUsers' => $totalActiveUsers,\n
        ]);\n

    final public function getApiRoles(): void\n

    #[OA\Get(\n
        path: '/api/user/{userId}',\n
        summary: 'Get user by ID (JSON)',\n
        tags: ['Users'],\n
        parameters: [\n

        ]\n

    final public function getApiUser(string $userId): void\n
    {\n
        $userRepo = new Repository(User::class);\n
        $utilisateur = $userRepo->getById($userId);\n
\n
        if ($utilisateur === null) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Utilisateur introuvable', 404);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $this->jsonSuccess($utilisateur->toArray());\n
