    #[OA\Post(\n
        path: '/api/add/user',\n
        summary: 'Add new user (JSON)',\n
        requestBody: new OA\RequestBody(\n
            required: true,\n
            content: new OA\JsonContent(\n
                required: ['firstname', 'lastname', 'email', 'password'],\n
                properties: [\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'firstname', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'lastname', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'email', type: 'string', format: 'email'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'password', type: 'string', format: 'password'),\n
                ]\n
            )\n
        ),\n
        tags: ['Users'],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 201, description: 'User created'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 400, description: 'Invalid input'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function addApiUser(): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        $donnees = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true);\n
\n
        $champsManquants = empty($donnees['firstname'])\n
            || empty($donnees['lastname'])\n
            || empty($donnees['email'])\n
            || empty($donnees['password'])\n
            || empty($donnees['roleId']);\n
\n
        if ($champsManquants) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Les champs prénom, nom, email, mot de passe et rôle sont obligatoires');\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if (!filter_var($donnees['email'], FILTER_VALIDATE_EMAIL)) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Format d\'email invalide');\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $userRepo = new Repository(User::class);\n
        $emailNormalise = trim(strtolower($donnees['email']));\n
        $utilisateurExistant = $userRepo->getByAttributes(['email' => $emailNormalise], false, null);\n
\n
        if ($utilisateurExistant !== null) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Un utilisateur avec cet email existe déjà', 409);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $nouvelUtilisateur = new User();\n
        $nouvelUtilisateur->setFirstname($donnees['firstname']);\n
        $nouvelUtilisateur->setLastname($donnees['lastname']);\n
        $nouvelUtilisateur->setEmail($emailNormalise);\n
        $nouvelUtilisateur->setPassword(password_hash($donnees['password'], PASSWORD_ARGON2I));\n
        $nouvelUtilisateur->setRoleId($donnees['roleId']);\n
        $nouvelUtilisateur->setCreatedat((new \DateTime())->format('Y-m-d H:i:s'));\n
\n
        $adminConnecte = Security::getUser();\n
        if ($adminConnecte !== null) {\n
            $nouvelUtilisateur->setCreatedby($adminConnecte->getId());\n
        }\n
\n
        $userRepo->insert($nouvelUtilisateur);\n
\n
        $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Utilisateur créé avec succès'], 201);\n
    }\n
\n
    #[OA\Patch(\n
        path: '/api/edit/user/{userId}',\n
        summary: 'Edit user (JSON)',\n
        tags: ['Users'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'userId', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n
        ],\n
        requestBody: new OA\RequestBody(\n
            required: true,\n
            content: new OA\JsonContent(\n
                properties: [\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'firstname', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'lastname', type: 'string'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'email', type: 'string', format: 'email'),\n
                ]\n
            )\n
        ),\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'User updated'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 403, description: 'Forbidden'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function editApiUser(string $userId): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        $userRepo = new Repository(User::class);\n
        $utilisateur = $userRepo->getById($userId);\n
\n
        if ($utilisateur === null) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Utilisateur introuvable', 404);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $donnees = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true);\n
\n
        if (!empty($donnees['firstname'])) {\n
            $utilisateur->setFirstname($donnees['firstname']);\n
        }\n
        if (!empty($donnees['lastname'])) {\n
            $utilisateur->setLastname($donnees['lastname']);\n
        }\n
        if (!empty($donnees['email'])) {\n
            if (!filter_var($donnees['email'], FILTER_VALIDATE_EMAIL)) {\n
                $this->jsonError('Format d\'email invalide');\n
                return;\n
            }\n
            $utilisateur->setEmail(trim(strtolower($donnees['email'])));\n
        }\n
        if (!empty($donnees['roleId'])) {\n
//            $adminConnecteCheck = Security::getUser();\n
//            // Un ADMIN ne peut pas assigner le rôle PDG\n
//            $roleRepo    = new Repository(Role::class);\n
//            $targetRole  = $roleRepo->getById($donnees['roleId']);\n
//            $targetRoleName = $targetRole?->getName() ?? '';\n
//            if ($adminConnecteCheck !== null\n
//                && $adminConnecteCheck->getRoleName() === 'ADMIN'\n
//                && strtoupper($targetRoleName) === 'PDG') {\n
//                $this->jsonError('Un administrateur ne peut pas attribuer le rôle PDG.', 403);\n
//                return;\n
//            }\n
            $utilisateur->setRoleId($donnees['roleId']);\n
        }\n
        if (array_key_exists('jobtitle', $donnees)) {\n
            $utilisateur->setJobtitle($donnees['jobtitle'] ?: null);\n
        }\n
        if (array_key_exists('fieldofwork', $donnees)) {\n
            $utilisateur->setFieldofwork($donnees['fieldofwork'] ?: null);\n
        }\n
        if (array_key_exists('degree', $donnees)) {\n
            $degree = $donnees['degree'];\n
            $utilisateur->setDegree(is_array($degree) ? array_filter($degree) : null);\n
        }\n
\n
        $utilisateur->setUpdatedat((new \DateTime())->format('Y-m-d H:i:s'));\n
\n
        $adminConnecte = Security::getUser();\n
        if ($adminConnecte !== null) {\n
            $utilisateur->setUpdatedby($adminConnecte->getId());\n
        }\n
\n
        $userRepo->update($utilisateur);\n
\n
        $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Utilisateur modifié avec succès']);\n
    }\n
\n
    #[OA\Post(\n
        path: '/api/change-password',\n
        summary: 'Change current user password',\n
        requestBody: new OA\RequestBody(\n
            required: true,\n
            content: new OA\JsonContent(\n
                required: ['currentPassword', 'newPassword'],\n
                properties: [\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'currentPassword', type: 'string', format: 'password'),\n
                    new OA\Property(property: 'newPassword', type: 'string', format: 'password'),\n
                ]\n
            )\n
        ),\n
        tags: ['Users'],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'Password changed'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 400, description: 'Validation error'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 401, description: 'Current password incorrect'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function changePassword(): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
        if (!$currentUser) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Non authentifié', 401);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $donnees = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true);\n
\n
        if (empty($donnees['currentPassword']) || empty($donnees['newPassword'])) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Les champs mot de passe actuel et nouveau mot de passe sont obligatoires');\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if (!password_verify($donnees['currentPassword'], $currentUser->getPassword())) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Mot de passe actuel incorrect', 401);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        if (strlen($donnees['newPassword']) < 8) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Le nouveau mot de passe doit contenir au moins 8 caractères');\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $userRepo = new Repository(User::class);\n
        $utilisateur = $userRepo->getById($currentUser->getId());\n
\n
        if (!$utilisateur) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Utilisateur introuvable', 404);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $utilisateur->setPassword(password_hash($donnees['newPassword'], PASSWORD_ARGON2I));\n
        $utilisateur->setUpdatedat((new \DateTime())->format('Y-m-d H:i:s'));\n
        $utilisateur->setUpdatedby($currentUser->getId());\n
\n
        $userRepo->update($utilisateur);\n
\n
        $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Mot de passe modifié avec succès']);\n
    }\n
\n
    #[OA\Delete(\n
        path: '/api/delete/user/{userId}',\n
        summary: 'Delete user (soft delete)',\n
        tags: ['Users'],\n
        parameters: [\n
            new OA\Parameter(name: 'userId', in: 'path', required: true, schema: new OA\Schema(type: 'string', format: 'uuid')),\n
        ],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'User deactivated'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 403, description: 'Forbidden'),\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function deleteApiUser(string $userId): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        $adminConnecte = Security::getUser();\n
\n
        // Empêcher l'auto-suppression (utiliser /api/delete/my-account à la place)\n
        if ($adminConnecte !== null && $adminConnecte->getId() === $userId) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Vous ne pouvez pas désactiver votre propre compte via cette route.', 403);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        $userRepo = new Repository(User::class);\n
        $utilisateur = $userRepo->getById($userId);\n
\n
        if ($utilisateur === null) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Utilisateur introuvable', 404);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        // Un ADMIN ne peut pas désactiver un PDG\n
        if ($adminConnecte !== null\n
            && $adminConnecte->getRoleName() === 'ADMIN'\n
            && $utilisateur->getRoleName() === 'PDG') {\n
            $this->jsonError('Un administrateur ne peut pas désactiver un PDG.', 403);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        // Soft delete : on désactive sans supprimer physiquement\n
        $utilisateur->setIsactive(false);\n
        //A la place $utilisateurs->delete($utilisateur)\n
        $utilisateur->setUpdatedat((new \DateTime())->format('Y-m-d H:i:s'));\n
\n
        if ($adminConnecte !== null) {\n
            $utilisateur->setUpdatedby($adminConnecte->getId());\n
        }\n
\n
        $userRepo->update($utilisateur);\n
\n
        $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Utilisateur désactivé avec succès']);\n
    }\n
\n
    #[OA\Delete(\n
        path: '/api/delete/my-account',\n
        summary: 'Delete current user account',\n
        tags: ['Users'],\n
        responses: [\n
            new OA\Response(response: 200, description: 'User account deleted successfully'),\n
            new OA\Response(response: 401, description: 'Unauthorized')\n
        ]\n
    )]\n
    final public function deleteMyAccount(): void\n
    {\n
        $this->verifyCsrf();\n
        $currentUser = Security::getUser();\n
        if (!$currentUser) {\n
            $this->jsonError('Non authentifié', 401);\n
            return;\n
        }\n
\n
        try {\n
            $userId      = $currentUser->getId();\n
            $userRepo    = new UserRepository();\n
            $taskRepo    = new TaskRepository();\n
            $projectRepo = new ProjectRepository();\n
\n
            $safe = function (callable $fn): void {\n
                try {\n
                    $fn();\n
                } catch (\PDOException $e) {\n
                    $code = $e->getCode();\n
                    if ($code !== '42703' && $code !== '42P01') {\n
                        throw $e;\n
                    }\n
                } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
                    if (strpos($e->getMessage(), 'SQLSTATE[42703]') === false && strpos($e->getMessage(), 'SQLSTATE[42P01]') === false) {\n
                        throw $e;\n
                    }\n
                }\n
            };\n
\n
            $safe(fn () => $projectRepo->nullifyManagerReferences($userId));\n
            $safe(fn () => $projectRepo->nullifyUserReferences($userId));\n
            $safe(fn () => $taskRepo->nullifyDeveloperReferences($userId));\n
            $safe(fn () => $taskRepo->deleteAllUserAssignments($userId));\n
            $safe(fn () => $userRepo->deleteAddressReferences($userId));\n
\n
            $userRepo->delete($userId);\n
\n
            Security::disconnect();\n
            setcookie('jwt_token', '', [\n
                'expires'  => time() - 3600,\n
                'path'     => '/',\n
                'httponly' => true,\n
                'secure'   => ($_ENV['APP_ENV'] ?? 'development') === 'production',\n
                'samesite' => 'Lax',\n
            ]);\n
\n
            $this->jsonSuccess(['message' => 'Compte supprimé avec succès']);\n
        } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
            error_log('[UsersController::deleteMyAccount] Error: ' . $e->getMessage());\n
            $this->jsonError('Une erreur est survenue lors de la suppression du compte');\n
        }\n
    }\n
}\n
